L0001: """
L0002: ATR(Average True Range) 기반 동적 SL/TP 계산
L0003: - SL = 진입가 - (ATR × sl_multiplier)   기본 1.5×
L0004: - TP = 진입가 + (ATR × tp_multiplier)   기본 3.0×
L0005: - 손익비 2:1 이상 유지
L0006: - 14봉 ATR (Wilder 방식)
L0007: """
L0008: import numpy as np
L0009: import pandas as pd
L0010: from dataclasses import dataclass
L0011: from utils.logger import logger
L0012: @dataclass
L0013: class StopLevels:
L0014:     stop_loss:   float
L0015:     take_profit: float
L0016:     atr:         float
L0017:     sl_pct:      float
L0018:     tp_pct:      float
L0019:     rr_ratio:    float
L0020: COIN_ATR_PROFILES = {
L0021:     "KRW-BTC":  {"min_sl": 0.010, "max_sl": 0.025, "sl_mult": 1.5, "tp_mult": 3.0},
L0022:     "KRW-ETH":  {"min_sl": 0.012, "max_sl": 0.028, "sl_mult": 1.5, "tp_mult": 3.0},
L0023:     "KRW-XRP":  {"min_sl": 0.015, "max_sl": 0.035, "sl_mult": 2.0, "tp_mult": 4.0},
L0024:     "KRW-SOL":  {"min_sl": 0.015, "max_sl": 0.035, "sl_mult": 2.0, "tp_mult": 4.0},
L0025:     "KRW-DOGE": {"min_sl": 0.018, "max_sl": 0.040, "sl_mult": 2.0, "tp_mult": 4.0},
L0026:     "KRW-AVAX": {"min_sl": 0.018, "max_sl": 0.038, "sl_mult": 2.0, "tp_mult": 4.0},
L0027:     "KRW-LINK": {"min_sl": 0.018, "max_sl": 0.038, "sl_mult": 2.0, "tp_mult": 4.0},
L0028:     "KRW-ATOM": {"min_sl": 0.018, "max_sl": 0.038, "sl_mult": 2.0, "tp_mult": 4.0},
L0029:     "KRW-DOT":  {"min_sl": 0.018, "max_sl": 0.038, "sl_mult": 2.0, "tp_mult": 4.0},
L0030:     "KRW-ADA":  {"min_sl": 0.018, "max_sl": 0.038, "sl_mult": 2.0, "tp_mult": 4.0},
L0031:     "KRW-SHIB": {"min_sl": 0.020, "max_sl": 0.045, "sl_mult": 2.0, "tp_mult": 4.0},
L0032:     "DEFAULT":  {"min_sl": 0.015, "max_sl": 0.035, "sl_mult": 2.0, "tp_mult": 4.0},
L0033:     "PENNY":    {"min_sl": 0.015, "max_sl": 0.030, "sl_mult": 1.5, "tp_mult": 4.5},
L0034: }
L0035: class ATRStopLoss:
L0036:     """
L0037:     ATR 기반 동적 손절/익절 계산기
L0038:     사용법:
L0039:         atr_sl = ATRStopLoss()
L0040:         levels = atr_sl.calculate(df, entry_price=121600)
L0041:         print(levels.stop_loss, levels.take_profit)
L0042:     """
L0043:     ATR_PERIOD    = 14
L0044:     SL_MULTIPLIER = 1.5
L0045:     TP_MULTIPLIER = 3.0
L0046:     MIN_SL_PCT    = 0.005
L0047:     MAX_SL_PCT    = 0.08
L0048:     def __init__(
L0049:         self,
L0050:         sl_multiplier: float = 1.5,
L0051:         tp_multiplier: float = 3.0,
L0052:     ):
L0053:         self.sl_mult = sl_multiplier
L0054:         self.tp_mult = tp_multiplier
L0055:     def calculate(self, df: pd.DataFrame, entry_price: float,
L0056:                   market: str = "") -> StopLevels:
L0057:         """
L0058:         df: OHLCV DataFrame (columns: open, high, low, close, volume)
L0059:         entry_price: 매수 진입가
L0060:         market: 코인 마켓명 (코인별 프로필 적용)
L0061:         Returns: StopLevels 데이터클래스
L0062:         """
L0063:         atr = self._calc_atr(df)
L0064:         if entry_price < 1.0:
L0065:             profile = COIN_ATR_PROFILES.get("PENNY", COIN_ATR_PROFILES["DEFAULT"])
L0066:         else:
L0067:             profile = COIN_ATR_PROFILES.get(market, COIN_ATR_PROFILES["DEFAULT"])
L0068:         sl_mult = profile["sl_mult"]
L0069:         tp_mult = profile["tp_mult"]
L0070:         min_sl  = profile["min_sl"]
L0071:         max_sl  = profile["max_sl"]
L0072:         raw_sl_dist = atr * sl_mult
L0073:         raw_tp_dist = atr * tp_mult
L0074:         sl_dist = max(
L0075:             entry_price * min_sl,
L0076:             min(raw_sl_dist, entry_price * max_sl),
L0077:         )
L0078:         tp_dist = sl_dist * (tp_mult / sl_mult)
L0079:         stop_loss   = entry_price - sl_dist
L0080:         take_profit = entry_price + tp_dist
L0081:         sl_pct = -sl_dist / entry_price
L0082:         tp_pct =  tp_dist / entry_price
L0083:         rr     = tp_dist  / sl_dist if sl_dist > 0 else 2.0
L0084:         logger.debug(
L0085:             f"[ATR-SL] entry={entry_price:.2f} ATR={atr:.4f} "
L0086:             f"SL={stop_loss:.2f}({sl_pct*100:.2f}%) "
L0087:             f"TP={take_profit:.2f}({tp_pct*100:.2f}%) "
L0088:             f"RR={rr:.2f}"
L0089:         )
L0090:         return StopLevels(
L0091:             stop_loss=stop_loss,
L0092:             take_profit=take_profit,
L0093:             atr=atr,
L0094:             sl_pct=sl_pct,
L0095:             tp_pct=tp_pct,
L0096:             rr_ratio=rr,
L0097:         )
L0098:     def _calc_atr(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> float:
L0099:         """Wilder ATR 계산 (14봉)"""
L0100:         if len(df) < self.ATR_PERIOD + 1:
L0101:             recent = df.tail(min(5, len(df)))
L0102:             hl_range = (recent["high"] - recent["low"]).mean()
L0103:             return float(hl_range) if not pd.isna(hl_range) else 0.0
L0104:         high  = df["high"].values.astype(float)
L0105:         low   = df["low"].values.astype(float)
L0106:         close = df["close"].values.astype(float)
L0107:         tr = np.maximum(
L0108:             high[1:] - low[1:],
L0109:             np.maximum(
L0110:                 np.abs(high[1:] - close[:-1]),
L0111:                 np.abs(low[1:]  - close[:-1]),
L0112:             ),
L0113:         )
L0114:         n   = self.ATR_PERIOD
L0115:         atr = np.zeros(len(tr))
L0116:         if len(tr) >= n:
L0117:             atr[n - 1] = tr[:n].mean()
L0118:             for i in range(n, len(tr)):
L0119:                 atr[i] = (atr[i - 1] * (n - 1) + tr[i]) / n
L0120:         last_atr = atr[-1]
L0121:         return float(last_atr) if last_atr > 0 else float(tr[-1]) if len(tr) > 0 else 0.0
L0122:     def get_dynamic_levels(
L0123:         self,
L0124:         df: pd.DataFrame,
L0125:         entry_price: float,
L0126:         current_price: float,
L0127:         profit_pct: float,
L0128:     ) -> StopLevels:
L0129:         """
L0130:         수익 구간별 SL/TP 동적 조정
L0131:         - 수익 +3% 이상: SL을 진입가(BEP)로 이동 (리스크 프리)
L0132:         - 수익 +5% 이상: SL을 +2%로 이동 (수익 보전)
L0133:         """
L0134:         levels = self.calculate(df, entry_price)
L0135:         if profit_pct >= 0.05:
L0136:             new_sl = entry_price * 1.02
L0137:             levels = StopLevels(
L0138:                 stop_loss   = max(levels.stop_loss, new_sl),
L0139:                 take_profit = levels.take_profit,
L0140:                 atr         = levels.atr,
L0141:                 sl_pct      = (max(levels.stop_loss, new_sl) - entry_price) / entry_price,
L0142:                 tp_pct      = levels.tp_pct,
L0143:                 rr_ratio    = levels.rr_ratio,
L0144:             )
L0145:             logger.debug(f"[ATR-SL] 수익보전 SL 이동: {new_sl:.2f} (+2%)")
L0146:         elif profit_pct >= 0.03:
L0147:             new_sl = entry_price * 1.001
L0148:             levels = StopLevels(
L0149:                 stop_loss   = max(levels.stop_loss, new_sl),
L0150:                 take_profit = levels.take_profit,
L0151:                 atr         = levels.atr,
L0152:                 sl_pct      = (max(levels.stop_loss, new_sl) - entry_price) / entry_price,
L0153:                 tp_pct      = levels.tp_pct,
L0154:                 rr_ratio    = levels.rr_ratio,
L0155:             )
L0156:             logger.debug(f"[ATR-SL] BEP SL 이동: {new_sl:.2f}")
L0157:         return levels

FILE: risk/stop_loss/trailing_stop.py  (4.5KB → 4.0KB)

L0001: """
L0002: 수익 +2% 달성 후 고점 대비 -1.5% 하락시 매도 트리거
L0003: - 포지션별 고점(peak_price) 추적
L0004: - _check()를 메인 루프 사이클마다 호출
L0005: """
L0006: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
L0007: from typing import Dict, Optional
L0008: from utils.logger import logger
L0009: @dataclass
L0010: class TrailingState:
L0011:     market:       str
L0012:     entry_price:  float
L0013:     peak_price:   float
L0014:     activated:    bool  = False
L0015:     trail_price:  float = 0.0
L0016: class TrailingStopManager:
L0017:     """
L0018:     포지션별 트레일링 스탑 상태 관리
L0019:     """
L0020:     ACTIVATE_PCT  = 0.02
L0021:     TRAIL_PCT     = 0.015
L0022:     def __init__(self):
L0023:         self._states: Dict[str, TrailingState] = {}
L0024:     def register(self, market: str, entry_price: float):
L0025:         """신규 포지션 등록"""
L0026:         self._states[market] = TrailingState(
L0027:             market=market,
L0028:             entry_price=entry_price,
L0029:             peak_price=entry_price,
L0030:         )
L0031:         logger.debug(f"[Trail] 등록: {market} @ {entry_price}")
L0032:     def unregister(self, market: str):
L0033:         """포지션 종료시 해제"""
L0034:         self._states.pop(market, None)
L0035:     def update(self, market: str, current_price: float) -> Optional[str]:
L0036:         """
L0037:         가격 업데이트 및 트리거 확인
L0038:         Returns: "SELL" if trailing stop triggered, else None
L0039:         """
L0040:         state = self._states.get(market)
L0041:         if state is None:
L0042:             return None
L0043:         if current_price > state.peak_price:
L0044:             state.peak_price = current_price
L0045:         profit_pct = (current_price - state.entry_price) / state.entry_price
L0046:         if not state.activated and profit_pct >= self.ACTIVATE_PCT:
L0047:             state.activated   = True
L0048:             state.trail_price = state.peak_price * (1 - self.TRAIL_PCT)
L0049:             logger.info(
L0050:                 f"[Trail] ✅ 활성화: {market} "
L0051:                 f"수익={profit_pct*100:.2f}% "
L0052:                 f"trail_price={state.trail_price:.2f}"
L0053:             )
L0054:         if not state.activated:
L0055:             return None
L0056:         new_trail = state.peak_price * (1 - self.TRAIL_PCT)
L0057:         if new_trail > state.trail_price:
L0058:             state.trail_price = new_trail
L0059:         if current_price <= state.trail_price:
L0060:             drop_pct = (state.peak_price - current_price) / state.peak_price
L0061:             logger.info(
L0062:                 f"[Trail] 🔴 발동: {market} "
L0063:                 f"peak={state.peak_price:.2f} "
L0064:                 f"current={current_price:.2f} "
L0065:                 f"drop={drop_pct*100:.2f}%"
L0066:             )
L0067:             return "SELL"
L0068:         return None
L0069:     def add_position(
L0070:         self,
L0071:         market: str,
L0072:         entry_price: float,
L0073:         stop_loss: float = 0.0,
L0074:         atr: float = 0.0,
L0075:         initial_stop: float = 0.0,
L0076:         take_profit: float = 0.0,
L0077:         **kwargs,
L0078:     ):
L0079:         """
L0080:         engine.py 호환 별칭 — ATR 기반 초기 트레일 설정 포함
L0081:         - atr > 0 이면 ATR x 2.0 을 초기 트레일 폭으로 사용
L0082:         - stop_loss > 0 이면 초기 손절가로 사용
L0083:         """
L0084:         self.register(market, entry_price)
L0085:         state = self._states.get(market)
L0086:         if state and atr > 0:
L0087:             atr_trail = entry_price - (atr * 2.0)
L0088:             if stop_loss > 0:
L0089:                 state.trail_price = max(stop_loss, atr_trail)
L0090:             else:
L0091:                 state.trail_price = atr_trail
L0092:             logger.debug(
L0093:                 f"[Trail] ATR 초기 트레일 설정: {market} "
L0094:                 f"trail={state.trail_price:.2f} "
L0095:                 f"(ATR={atr:.2f} x 2.0)"
L0096:             )
L0097:         elif state and stop_loss > 0:
L0098:             state.trail_price = stop_loss
L0099:     def remove_position(self, market: str):
L0100:         """engine.py 호환 별칭 — unregister()와 동일"""
L0101:         self.unregister(market)
L0102:     def get_status(self, market: str) -> Optional[dict]:
L0103:         state = self._states.get(market)
L0104:         if not state:
L0105:             return None
L0106:         profit_pct = 0.0
L0107:         return {
L0108:             "activated":    state.activated,
L0109:             "peak_price":   state.peak_price,
L0110:             "trail_price":  state.trail_price,
L0111:             "entry_price":  state.entry_price,
L0112:         }

FILE: risk/position_sizer.py  (6.4KB → 5.3KB)

L0001: """
L0002: Half-Kelly Criterion 기반 동적 포지션 사이징
L0003: - 승률(W)과 손익비(R)를 DB 실거래 데이터에서 자동 계산
L0004: - 초기(데이터 부족) 구간은 고정 비율 fallback
L0005: - 최대 리스크 캡: 총자산의 5% (단일 포지션)
L0006: - 최소 주문금액: 5,000 KRW (업비트 제한)
L0007: """
L0008: import sqlite3
L0009: from pathlib import Path
L0010: from typing import Optional
L0011: from utils.logger import logger
L0012: class KellyPositionSizer:
L0013:     """
L0014:     Half-Kelly Criterion 포지션 사이저
L0015:     - min_trades 이상 데이터 있을 때 Kelly 활성화
L0016:     - 그 이전엔 fixed_ratio 고정 비율 사용
L0017:     """
L0018:     MIN_TRADES       = 20
L0019:     HALF_KELLY       = 0.5
L0020:     MAX_RISK_PCT     = 0.05
L0021:     MIN_RISK_PCT     = 0.01
L0022:     FIXED_RATIO      = 0.02
L0023:     MIN_ORDER_KRW    = 5_000
L0024:     DB_PATH          = Path("database/apex_bot.db")
L0025:     STRATEGY_MULTIPLIER = {
L0026:         "BEAR_REVERSAL":     1.2,
L0027:         "OrderBlock_SMC":    1.0,
L0028:         "VWAP_Reversion":    0.9,
L0029:         "volatility_break":  1.1,
L0030:         "ml_signal":         1.3,
L0031:         "default":           1.0,
L0032:     }
L0033:     def __init__(self, db_path: Optional[Path] = None):
L0034:         self.db_path = db_path or self.DB_PATH
L0035:         self._cache: dict = {}
L0036:         self._cache_count: int = 0
L0037:     def calculate(
L0038:         self,
L0039:         total_capital: float,
L0040:         strategy: str = "default",
L0041:         market: str = "",
L0042:         confidence: float = 0.5,
L0043:     ) -> float:
L0044:         """
L0045:         Returns: 매수 금액 (KRW), 최소 MIN_ORDER_KRW 보장
L0046:         """
L0047:         kelly_f = self._get_kelly_fraction(strategy)
L0048:         base_amount = total_capital * kelly_f
L0049:         conf_multiplier = 0.7 + (confidence * 0.6)
L0050:         base_amount *= conf_multiplier
L0051:         strat_mul = self.STRATEGY_MULTIPLIER.get(
L0052:             strategy, self.STRATEGY_MULTIPLIER["default"]
L0053:         )
L0054:         base_amount *= strat_mul
L0055:         max_amount = total_capital * self.MAX_RISK_PCT
L0056:         min_amount = max(total_capital * self.MIN_RISK_PCT, self.MIN_ORDER_KRW)
L0057:         amount = max(min_amount, min(base_amount, max_amount))
L0058:         logger.info(
L0059:             f"[Kelly] {strategy} {market} | "
L0060:             f"kelly_f={kelly_f:.4f} conf={confidence:.2f} "
L0061:             f"strat_mul={strat_mul} → ₩{amount:,.0f}"
L0062:         )
L0063:         return amount
L0064:     def _get_kelly_fraction(self, strategy: str) -> float:
L0065:         """DB 거래 이력 기반 Half-Kelly f* 계산"""
L0066:         self._cache_count += 1
L0067:         if strategy in self._cache and self._cache_count % 20 != 0:
L0068:             return self._cache[strategy]
L0069:         try:
L0070:             stats = self._query_stats(strategy)
L0071:             if stats is None or stats["total"] < self.MIN_TRADES:
L0072:                 logger.debug(
L0073:                     f"[Kelly] {strategy}: 데이터 부족 "
L0074:                     f"({stats['total'] if stats else 0}건) "
L0075:                     f"→ 고정 {self.FIXED_RATIO*100:.0f}%"
L0076:                 )
L0077:                 return self.FIXED_RATIO
L0078:             W = stats["win_rate"]
L0079:             R = stats["rr_ratio"]
L0080:             raw_kelly = (W * R - (1 - W)) / R
L0081:             half_kelly = max(raw_kelly * self.HALF_KELLY, self.MIN_RISK_PCT)
L0082:             capped     = min(half_kelly, self.MAX_RISK_PCT)
L0083:             self._cache[strategy] = capped
L0084:             logger.info(
L0085:                 f"[Kelly] {strategy}: W={W:.2f} R={R:.2f} "
L0086:                 f"raw={raw_kelly:.4f} half={half_kelly:.4f} "
L0087:                 f"→ capped={capped:.4f} ({capped*100:.2f}%)"
L0088:             )
L0089:             return capped
L0090:         except Exception as e:
L0091:             logger.warning(f"[Kelly] 계산 실패({strategy}): {e}")
L0092:             return self.FIXED_RATIO
L0093:     def _query_stats(self, strategy: str) -> Optional[dict]:
L0094:         """SQLite trade_history에서 승률·손익비 계산"""
L0095:         if not self.db_path.exists():
L0096:             return None
L0097:         con = sqlite3.connect(str(self.db_path))
L0098:         cur = con.cursor()
L0099:         try:
L0100:             if strategy != "default":
L0101:                 cur.execute(
L0102:                     """
L0103:                     SELECT profit_rate FROM trade_history
L0104:                     WHERE side='SELL' AND strategy=?
L0105:                     ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 100
L0106:                     """,
L0107:                     (strategy,),
L0108:                 )
L0109:             else:
L0110:                 cur.execute(
L0111:                     """
L0112:                     SELECT profit_rate FROM trade_history
L0113:                     WHERE side='SELL'
L0114:                     ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 100
L0115:                     """
L0116:                 )
L0117:             rows = [r[0] for r in cur.fetchall()]
L0118:         finally:
L0119:             con.close()
L0120:         if not rows:
L0121:             return {"total": 0, "win_rate": 0, "rr_ratio": 1}
L0122:         wins   = [r for r in rows if r > 0]
L0123:         losses = [r for r in rows if r <= 0]
L0124:         total  = len(rows)
L0125:         W      = len(wins) / total if total else 0
L0126:         avg_win  = sum(wins)   / len(wins)   if wins   else 0.001
L0127:         avg_loss = abs(sum(losses) / len(losses)) if losses else 0.001
L0128:         R        = avg_win / avg_loss if avg_loss > 0 else 1.0
L0129:         return {"total": total, "win_rate": W, "rr_ratio": R}
L0130:     def get_summary(self) -> str:
L0131:         """현재 Kelly 계수 요약 출력"""
L0132:         lines = ["[Kelly Criterion 현황]"]
L0133:         for strat, f in self._cache.items():
L0134:             lines.append(f"  {strat}: {f*100:.2f}%")
L0135:         if not self._cache:
L0136:             lines.append(f"  데이터 부족 → 전략 고정 {self.FIXED_RATIO*100:.0f}%")
L0137:         return "\n".join(lines)

FILE: risk/partial_exit.py  (6.2KB → 5.7KB)

L0001: """
L0002: APEX BOT - 부분 청산 (Partial Exit) 관리자
L0003: 목표가 도달 시 포지션 일부 익절 → 나머지는 트레일링으로 수익 극대화
L0004: 청산 단계:
L0005:   Step 1: 목표가 50% 도달 → 25% 청산 (수익 확정)
L0006:   Step 2: 목표가 100% 도달 → 50% 청산 (익절)
L0007:   Step 3: 목표가 150% 도달 → 25% 청산 (추가 익절)
L0008:   나머지: 트레일링 스탑으로 계속 추적
L0009: """
L0010: from __future__ import annotations
L0011: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
L0012: from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
L0013: from loguru import logger
L0014: @dataclass
L0015: class PartialExitLevel:
L0016:     """개별 청산 단계"""
L0017:     profit_pct: float
L0018:     exit_ratio: float
L0019:     executed: bool = False
L0020: @dataclass
L0021: class PartialExitState:
L0022:     """포지션별 부분 청산 상태"""
L0023:     market: str
L0024:     entry_price: float
L0025:     initial_volume: float
L0026:     remaining_volume: float
L0027:     take_profit: float
L0028:     levels: List[PartialExitLevel] = field(default_factory=list)
L0029:     total_exited_ratio: float = 0.0
L0030:     def __post_init__(self):
L0031:         if not self.levels:
L0032:             tp_range = self.take_profit - self.entry_price
L0033:             if tp_range <= 0:
L0034:                 tp_range = self.entry_price * 0.05
L0035:             self.levels = [
L0036:                 PartialExitLevel(
L0037:                     profit_pct=(self.entry_price * 1 + tp_range * 0.5 - self.entry_price)
L0038:                                / self.entry_price,
L0039:                     exit_ratio=0.25,
L0040:                 ),
L0041:                 PartialExitLevel(
L0042:                     profit_pct=(self.entry_price + tp_range * 1.0 - self.entry_price)
L0043:                                / self.entry_price,
L0044:                     exit_ratio=0.50,
L0045:                 ),
L0046:                 PartialExitLevel(
L0047:                     profit_pct=(self.entry_price + tp_range * 1.5 - self.entry_price)
L0048:                                / self.entry_price,
L0049:                     exit_ratio=0.25,
L0050:                 ),
L0051:             ]
L0052: class PartialExitManager:
L0053:     """
L0054:     부분 청산 관리자
L0055:     엔진 연동 방법:
L0056:         partial_exit.add_position(market, entry_price, volume, take_profit)
L0057:         exit_vol = partial_exit.check(market, current_price)
L0058:         if exit_vol > 0:
L0059:             await executor.execute(sell partial exit_vol)
L0060:         partial_exit.remove_position(market)
L0061:     """
L0062:     def __init__(self):
L0063:         self._positions: Dict[str, PartialExitState] = {}
L0064:     def add_position(
L0065:         self,
L0066:         market: str,
L0067:         entry_price: float,
L0068:         volume: float,
L0069:         take_profit: float,
L0070:         custom_levels: Optional[List[Tuple[float, float]]] = None,
L0071:     ):
L0072:         """
L0073:         포지션 추가
L0074:         Args:
L0075:             market:       마켓 코드 (예: KRW-BTC)
L0076:             entry_price:  진입가
L0077:             volume:       매수 수량
L0078:             take_profit:  목표가 (100% 달성 기준)
L0079:             custom_levels: [(수익률, 청산비율), ...] 커스텀 단계
L0080:         """
L0081:         if entry_price <= 0 or volume <= 0:
L0082:             return
L0083:         state = PartialExitState(
L0084:             market=market,
L0085:             entry_price=entry_price,
L0086:             initial_volume=volume,
L0087:             remaining_volume=volume,
L0088:             take_profit=take_profit,
L0089:         )
L0090:         if custom_levels:
L0091:             state.levels = [
L0092:                 PartialExitLevel(profit_pct=pct, exit_ratio=ratio)
L0093:                 for pct, ratio in custom_levels
L0094:             ]
L0095:         self._positions[market] = state
L0096:         logger.debug(
L0097:             f"📊 부분청산 설정 | {market} | 진입={entry_price:,.0f} | "
L0098:             f"목표={take_profit:,.0f} | {len(state.levels)}단계"
L0099:         )
L0100:     def check(self, market: str, current_price: float) -> float:
L0101:         """
L0102:         가격 업데이트 → 청산 수량 반환
L0103:         Returns:
L0104:             청산할 코인 수량 (0이면 청산 없음)
L0105:         """
L0106:         state = self._positions.get(market)
L0107:         if not state or state.remaining_volume <= 0:
L0108:             return 0.0
L0109:         current_return = (current_price - state.entry_price) / state.entry_price
L0110:         for level in state.levels:
L0111:             if level.executed:
L0112:                 continue
L0113:             if current_return >= level.profit_pct:
L0114:                 exit_volume = state.initial_volume * level.exit_ratio
L0115:                 exit_volume = min(exit_volume, state.remaining_volume)
L0116:                 if exit_volume <= 0:
L0117:                     continue
L0118:                 level.executed = True
L0119:                 state.remaining_volume -= exit_volume
L0120:                 state.total_exited_ratio += level.exit_ratio
L0121:                 logger.info(
L0122:                     f"💰 부분 청산 발동 | {market} | "
L0123:                     f"수익률={current_return:.2%} ≥ 목표={level.profit_pct:.2%} | "
L0124:                     f"청산={exit_volume:.6f} ({level.exit_ratio:.0%}) | "
L0125:                     f"잔량={state.remaining_volume:.6f}"
L0126:                 )
L0127:                 return exit_volume
L0128:         return 0.0
L0129:     def get_remaining_volume(self, market: str) -> float:
L0130:         """남은 포지션 수량"""
L0131:         state = self._positions.get(market)
L0132:         return state.remaining_volume if state else 0.0
L0133:     def get_exited_ratio(self, market: str) -> float:
L0134:         """누적 청산 비율"""
L0135:         state = self._positions.get(market)
L0136:         return state.total_exited_ratio if state else 0.0
L0137:     def remove_position(self, market: str):
L0138:         """포지션 제거"""
L0139:         self._positions.pop(market, None)
L0140:     def get_state(self, market: str) -> Optional[PartialExitState]:
L0141:         return self._positions.get(market)
L0142:     def get_all_states(self) -> Dict[str, PartialExitState]:
L0143:         return self._positions.copy()
L0144:     def pending_levels(self, market: str) -> int:
L0145:         """미실행 청산 단계 수"""
L0146:         state = self._positions.get(market)
L0147:         if not state:
L0148:             return 0
L0149:         return sum(1 for lv in state.levels if not lv.executed)

L0104:         if len(self._trade_results) < 10:
L0105:             return {"win_rate": 0.5, "avg_win": 0.02, "avg_loss": 0.01}
L0106:         wins = sum(self._trade_results)

L0115:             return 0.0
L0116:         recent = self._trade_results[-10:]
L0117:         return sum(recent) / len(recent) * 100

L0128:         )

L0132:         )

L0066:     def remove_position(self, market: str):

L0068:     def check_exit(self, market: str, current_price: float) -> ExitSignal:
L0069:         """포지션 청산 조건 체크"""
L0070:         pos = self.positions.get(market)
L0071:         if pos is None:
L0072:             return ExitSignal(False, ExitReason.SIGNAL_SELL)
L0073:         pnl = (current_price - pos.entry_price) / pos.entry_price
L0074:         pos.max_price = max(pos.max_price, current_price)
L0075:         if current_price <= pos.stop_loss:
L0076:             return ExitSignal(True, ExitReason.STOP_LOSS, 1.0,
L0077:                 f"손절: {pnl:.2%}")
L0078:         if pnl >= self.breakeven_trigger and not pos.breakeven_set:
L0079:             pos.stop_loss   = pos.entry_price * 1.001
L0080:             pos.breakeven_set = True

L0082:         if pnl >= self.partial_exit_1 and not pos.partial_exited:
L0083:             pos.partial_exited = True
L0084:             return ExitSignal(True, ExitReason.PARTIAL_EXIT,

L0087:         if pnl >= self.partial_exit_2 and pos.partial_exited:

L0089:                 f"2차 익절: {pnl:.2%}")
L0090:         held_hours = (datetime.now() - pos.entry_time).total_seconds() / 3600
L0091:         if held_hours >= self.max_hold_hours:
L0092:             return ExitSignal(True, ExitReason.TIME_EXIT, 1.0,
L0093:                 f"보유시간 초과: {held_hours:.1f}h")
L0094:         return ExitSignal(False, ExitReason.SIGNAL_SELL)
L0095:     def check_pyramid(self, market: str, current_price: float) -> Tuple[bool, float]:
L0096:         """피라미딩 추가진입 조건 체크 → (진입여부, 추가금액비율)"""
L0097:         pos = self.positions.get(market)
L0098:         if pos is None:
L0099:             return False, 0.0
L0100:         if pos.pyramid_count >= self.pyramid_max:
L0101:             return False, 0.0
L0102:         pnl = (current_price - pos.entry_price) / pos.entry_price
L0103:         if pnl >= self.pyramid_trigger * (pos.pyramid_count + 1):
L0104:             add_ratio = 0.5 ** (pos.pyramid_count + 1)
L0105:             pos.pyramid_count += 1
L0106:             logger.info(
L0107:                 f"📈 피라미딩 {pos.pyramid_count}/{self.pyramid_max} | "
L0108:                 f"{market} | 추가비율={add_ratio:.0%}"
L0109:             )
L0110:             return True, add_ratio
L0111:         return False, 0.0

L0113:         return self.positions.copy()

L0001: """
L0002: APEX BOT - 신호 결합기
L0003: 멀티 전략 신호 → 앙상블 최종 신호 생성
L0004: 수정 이력:
L0005:   v1.1 - _filter_by_regime() Signal 생성 인수 불일치 수정
L0006:          (signal_type= → signal=, strength= → score=)
L0007:        - 부스트 신호 생성 헬퍼 _boost_signal() 추가
L0008: """
L0009: import asyncio
L0010: from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
L0011: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
L0012: from datetime import datetime
L0013: import pandas as pd
L0014: from loguru import logger
L0015: from strategies.base_strategy import StrategySignal as Signal, SignalType
L0016: from config.settings import get_settings
L0017: @dataclass
L0018: class CombinedSignal:
L0019:     """앙상블 결합 최종 신호"""
L0020:     market: str
L0021:     signal_type: SignalType
L0022:     score: float
L0023:     confidence: float
L0024:     agreement_rate: float
L0025:     contributing_strategies: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
L0026:     reasons: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
L0027:     metadata: Dict = field(default_factory=dict)
L0028:     ml_signal: Optional[str] = None
L0029:     ml_confidence: float = 0.0
L0030: class SignalCombiner:
L0031:     """
L0032:     멀티 전략 신호 결합 엔진
L0033:     가중치 체계:
L0034:     - ML 앙상블 (LSTM+TFT+CNN): 가중치 2.5
L0035:     - 시장구조 (OB/SMC): 1.5
L0036:     - 모멘텀 (MACD/RSI/Supertrend): 1.0~1.5
L0037:     - 변동성 돌파 (ATR/볼린저): 1.0
L0038:     - 평균회귀 (VWAP/BB): 1.2
L0039:     """
L0040:     STRATEGY_WEIGHTS = {
L0041:         "MACD_Cross":        1.8,
L0042:         "RSI_Divergence":    0.0,
L0043:         "Supertrend":        1.3,
L0044:         "Bollinger_Squeeze": 1.0,
L0045:         "VWAP_Reversion":    1.2,
L0046:         "VolBreakout":       0.4,
L0047:         "ATR_Channel":       1.0,
L0048:         "OrderBlock_SMC":    0.3,
L0049:         "ML_Ensemble":       3.0,
L0050:         "BEAR_REVERSAL":     2.0,
L0051:     }
L0052:     REGIME_PREFERRED = {
L0053:         "TRENDING":   {"MACD_Cross", "Supertrend", "OrderBlock_SMC", "VolBreakout"},
L0054:         "RANGING":    {"VWAP_Reversion", "Bollinger_Squeeze", "RSI_Divergence", "ATR_Channel"},
L0055:         "VOLATILE":   {"VolBreakout", "ATR_Channel", "Bollinger_Squeeze"},
L0056:         "BEAR_REVERSAL": {"RSI_Divergence", "VWAP_Reversion", "Bollinger_Squeeze"},
L0057:     }
L0058:     def __init__(self, settings=None):
L0059:         self.settings = settings or get_settings()
L0060:         self.buy_threshold  = self.settings.risk.buy_signal_threshold
L0061:         self.sell_threshold = self.settings.risk.sell_signal_threshold
L0062:         self.min_agreement  = 0.20
L0063:     def combine(
L0064:         self,
L0065:         signals: List[Signal],
L0066:         market: str,
L0067:         ml_prediction: Optional[Dict] = None,
L0068:         regime: str = "UNKNOWN",
L0069:     ) -> Optional[CombinedSignal]:
L0070:         """다중 신호 결합 → 최종 신호 반환"""
L0071:         if not signals and not ml_prediction:
L0072:             return None
L0073:         ml_signal     = None
L0074:         ml_confidence = 0.0
L0075:         if ml_prediction:
L0076:             ml_signal     = ml_prediction.get("signal", "HOLD")
L0077:             ml_confidence = ml_prediction.get("confidence", 0.0)
L0078:         filtered_signals = self._filter_by_regime(signals, regime)
L0079:         buy_score  = 0.0
L0080:         sell_score = 0.0
L0081:         buy_strategies  = []
L0082:         sell_strategies = []
L0083:         reasons = []
L0084:         for sig in filtered_signals:
L0085:             weight           = self.STRATEGY_WEIGHTS.get(sig.strategy_name, 1.0)
L0086:             weighted_strength = sig.score * weight * sig.confidence
L0087:             if sig.signal == SignalType.BUY:
L0088:                 buy_score += weighted_strength
L0089:                 buy_strategies.append(sig.strategy_name)
L0090:                 reasons.append(sig.reason)
L0091:             elif sig.signal == SignalType.SELL:
L0092:                 sell_score += weighted_strength
L0093:                 sell_strategies.append(sig.strategy_name)
L0094:                 reasons.append(sig.reason)
L0095:         if ml_signal and ml_confidence > 0.50:
L0096:             ml_weight = self.STRATEGY_WEIGHTS["ML_Ensemble"]
L0097:             if ml_signal == "BUY":
L0098:                 buy_score += ml_weight * ml_confidence
L0099:                 buy_strategies.append("ML_Ensemble")
L0100:             elif ml_signal == "SELL":
L0101:                 sell_score += ml_weight * ml_confidence
L0102:                 sell_strategies.append("ML_Ensemble")
L0103:         total_strategies = len(filtered_signals) + (1 if ml_signal else 0)
L0104:         net_score        = buy_score - sell_score
L0105:         if net_score >= self.buy_threshold:
L0106:             n_buy          = len(buy_strategies)
L0107:             agreement_rate = n_buy / max(total_strategies, 1)
L0108:             if agreement_rate < self.min_agreement:
L0109:                 return None
L0110:             avg_confidence = (
L0111:                 sum(s.confidence for s in filtered_signals
L0112:                     if s.signal == SignalType.BUY)
L0113:                 / max(n_buy, 1)
L0114:             )
L0115:             return CombinedSignal(
L0116:                 market=market,
L0117:                 signal_type=SignalType.BUY,
L0118:                 score=buy_score,
L0119:                 confidence=avg_confidence,
L0120:                 agreement_rate=agreement_rate,
L0121:                 contributing_strategies=buy_strategies,
L0122:                 reasons=reasons[:5],
L0123:                 metadata={
L0124:                     "buy_score": buy_score,
L0125:                     "sell_score": sell_score,
L0126:                     "regime": regime,
L0127:                 },
L0128:                 ml_signal=ml_signal,
L0129:                 ml_confidence=ml_confidence,
L0130:             )
L0131:         elif net_score <= self.sell_threshold:
L0132:             n_sell         = len(sell_strategies)
L0133:             agreement_rate = n_sell / max(total_strategies, 1)
L0134:             if agreement_rate < self.min_agreement and not (
L0135:                 ml_signal == 'SELL' and ml_confidence > 0.55
L0136:             ):
L0137:                 return None
L0138:             avg_confidence = (
L0139:                 sum(s.confidence for s in filtered_signals
L0140:                     if s.signal == SignalType.SELL)
L0141:                 / max(n_sell, 1)
L0142:             )
L0143:             return CombinedSignal(
L0144:                 market=market,
L0145:                 signal_type=SignalType.SELL,
L0146:                 score=-sell_score,
L0147:                 confidence=avg_confidence,
L0148:                 agreement_rate=agreement_rate,
L0149:                 contributing_strategies=sell_strategies,
L0150:                 reasons=reasons[:5],
L0151:                 metadata={
L0152:                     "buy_score": buy_score,
L0153:                     "sell_score": sell_score,
L0154:                     "regime": regime,
L0155:                 },
L0156:                 ml_signal=ml_signal,
L0157:                 ml_confidence=ml_confidence,
L0158:             )
L0159:         return None
L0160:     def _filter_by_regime(
L0161:         self, signals: List[Signal], regime: str
L0162:     ) -> List[Signal]:
L0163:         """
L0164:         시장 레짐에 맞는 전략만 필터링 + 선호 전략 1.2배 부스트
L0165:         ✅ FIX: Signal 생성 시 signal= (not signal_type=),
L0166:                 score= (not strength=) 사용
L0167:         """
L0168:         preferred = self.REGIME_PREFERRED.get(regime.upper(), None)
L0169:         if preferred is None:
L0170:             return signals
L0171:         boosted = []
L0172:         for sig in signals:
L0173:             if sig.strategy_name in preferred:
L0174:                 boosted.append(
L0175:                     self._boost_signal(sig, score_mult=1.2, reason_suffix="[레짐부스트]")
L0176:                 )
L0177:             else:
L0178:                 boosted.append(sig)
L0179:         return boosted
L0180:     @staticmethod
L0181:     def _boost_signal(sig: Signal, score_mult: float = 1.0,
L0182:                       reason_suffix: str = "") -> Signal:
L0183:         """
L0184:         ✅ FIX: StrategySignal 실제 필드명(signal, score)으로 새 신호 생성
L0185:         """
L0186:         from strategies.base_strategy import StrategySignal
L0187:         return StrategySignal(
L0188:             strategy_name=sig.strategy_name,
L0189:             market=sig.market,
L0190:             signal=sig.signal,
L0191:             score=min(sig.score * score_mult, 1.0),
L0192:             confidence=sig.confidence,
L0193:             entry_price=sig.entry_price,
L0194:             stop_loss=sig.stop_loss,
L0195:             take_profit=sig.take_profit,
L0196:             reason=sig.reason + reason_suffix,
L0197:             timeframe=sig.timeframe,
L0198:             timestamp=sig.timestamp,
L0199:             metadata=sig.metadata,
L0200:         )
L0201:     def get_score_breakdown(self, signals: List[Signal]) -> Dict:
L0202:         """신호 점수 상세 내역"""
L0203:         breakdown = {}
L0204:         for sig in signals:
L0205:             weight = self.STRATEGY_WEIGHTS.get(sig.strategy_name, 1.0)
L0206:             breakdown[sig.strategy_name] = {
L0207:                 "type":           sig.signal.name,
L0208:                 "strength":       sig.score,
L0209:                 "confidence":     sig.confidence,
L0210:                 "weight":         weight,
L0211:                 "weighted_score": sig.score * weight * sig.confidence,
L0212:             }
L0213:         return breakdown

L0001: """
L0002: APEX BOT - 시장 레짐 감지기 v2.0
L0003: 추세/횡보/변동성/베어반전 국면 자동 분류
L0004: Step 3 고도화:
L0005:   - BEAR_REVERSAL 신규 레짐 추가
L0006:     조건: RSI≤28 + Fear&Greed≤20 + BB%≤0.05 중 2개 이상
L0007:     → 하락장이지만 극단적 과매도 → 역발상 매수 허용
L0008:   - 레짐별 허용 전략 세분화 (TRENDING_DOWN 완전 차단 해제)
L0009:   - 허스트 지수 계산 수치 안정화 (log(0) 방지)
L0010: """
L0011: import numpy as np
L0012: import pandas as pd
L0013: from typing import Dict, Optional, Tuple, List
L0014: from enum import Enum
L0015: from loguru import logger
L0016: class MarketRegime(Enum):
L0017:     TRENDING_UP    = "TRENDING_UP"
L0018:     TRENDING_DOWN  = "TRENDING_DOWN"
L0019:     RANGING        = "RANGING"
L0020:     VOLATILE       = "VOLATILE"
L0021:     BEAR_REVERSAL  = "BEAR_REVERSAL"
L0022:     UNKNOWN        = "UNKNOWN"
L0023: REGIME_ALLOWED_STRATEGIES: Dict[str, Optional[List[str]]] = {
L0024:     "TRENDING_UP":   None,
L0025:     "TRENDING_DOWN": [],
L0026:     "RANGING":       ["RSI_Divergence", "VWAP_Reversion",
L0027:                       "Bollinger_Squeeze", "ATR_Channel",
L0028:                       "ML_Ensemble"],
L0029:     "VOLATILE":      ["VolBreakout", "ATR_Channel",
L0030:                       "Bollinger_Squeeze", "ML_Ensemble"],
L0031:     "BEAR_REVERSAL": ["RSI_Divergence", "VWAP_Reversion",
L0032:                       "Bollinger_Squeeze", "ML_Ensemble"],
L0033:     "UNKNOWN":       None,
L0034: }
L0035: class RegimeDetector:
L0036:     """
L0037:     시장 레짐 자동 감지기
L0038:     사용 지표:
L0039:     - ADX: 추세 강도
L0040:     - ATR / 역사적 변동성: 변동성 측정
L0041:     - 볼린저 밴드 폭: 횡보 판단
L0042:     - 허스트 지수: 추세 vs 평균회귀 성향
L0043:     - EMA 정렬: 추세 방향
L0044:     - RSI + BB%: BEAR_REVERSAL 감지
L0045:     """
L0046:     def __init__(self):
L0047:         self.adx_trend_threshold  = 25
L0048:         self.adx_strong_threshold = 40
L0049:         self.vol_threshold        = 2.0
L0050:         self.bb_squeeze_threshold = 0.03
L0051:         self._cache: Dict[str, MarketRegime] = {}
L0052:         self._bear_reversal_counts: Dict[str, int] = {}
L0053:     def detect(
L0054:         self,
L0055:         market: str,
L0056:         df: pd.DataFrame,
L0057:         timeframe: str = "60",
L0058:         fear_greed_index: Optional[int] = None,
L0059:     ) -> MarketRegime:
L0060:         """
L0061:         시장 레짐 감지
L0062:         Args:
L0063:             fear_greed_index: 공포탐욕 지수 (BEAR_REVERSAL 감지용)
L0064:         """
L0065:         if df is None or len(df) < 50:
L0066:             return MarketRegime.UNKNOWN
L0067:         try:
L0068:             last  = df.iloc[-1]
L0069:             close = df["close"]
L0070:             adx      = float(last.get("adx",      0) or 0)
L0071:             di_plus  = float(last.get("di_plus",  0) or 0)
L0072:             di_minus = float(last.get("di_minus", 0) or 0)
L0073:             atr_pct  = float(last.get("atr_pct",  1) or 1)
L0074:             bb_width = float(last.get("bb_width", 0.05) or 0.05)
L0075:             bb_pct   = float(last.get("bb_pct",   0.5) or 0.5)
L0076:             rsi      = float(last.get("rsi",      50)  or 50)
L0077:             price    = float(close.iloc[-1])
L0078:             hist_vol = (
L0079:                 close.pct_change().rolling(20).std().iloc[-1] * np.sqrt(365) * 100
L0080:             )
L0081:             ema20  = float(last.get("ema20",  price) or price)
L0082:             ema50  = float(last.get("ema50",  price) or price)
L0083:             ema200 = float(last.get("ema200", price) or price)
L0084:             ema_bull = price > ema20 > ema50 > ema200
L0085:             ema_bear = price < ema20 < ema50 < ema200
L0086:             hurst = self._calc_hurst(close.tail(100))
L0087:             bear_reversal = self._check_bear_reversal(
L0088:                 rsi=rsi,
L0089:                 bb_pct=bb_pct,
L0090:                 fear_greed_index=fear_greed_index,
L0091:                 adx=adx,
L0092:                 di_minus=di_minus,
L0093:                 di_plus=di_plus,
L0094:             )
L0095:             if bear_reversal:
L0096:                 regime = MarketRegime.BEAR_REVERSAL
L0097:             else:
L0098:                 regime = self._classify(
L0099:                     adx=adx, di_plus=di_plus, di_minus=di_minus,
L0100:                     bb_width=bb_width, atr_pct=atr_pct,
L0101:                     historical_vol=hist_vol, hurst=hurst,
L0102:                     ema_bull_aligned=ema_bull,
L0103:                     ema_bear_aligned=ema_bear,
L0104:                     price=price, ema200=ema200,
L0105:                 )
L0106:             self._cache[market] = regime
L0107:             logger.debug(
L0108:                 f"레짐 감지 | {market} | {regime.value} | "
L0109:                 f"ADX={adx:.1f} BB폭={bb_width:.3f} "
L0110:                 f"허스트={hurst:.3f} RSI={rsi:.1f}"
L0111:                 + (f" FG={fear_greed_index}" if fear_greed_index else "")
L0112:             )
L0113:             return regime
L0114:         except Exception as e:
L0115:             logger.error(f"레짐 감지 오류 ({market}): {e}")
L0116:             return MarketRegime.UNKNOWN

L0181:     def _check_bear_reversal(
L0182:         self,
L0183:         rsi: float,
L0184:         bb_pct: float,
L0185:         fear_greed_index: Optional[int],
L0186:         adx: float,
L0187:         di_minus: float,
L0188:         di_plus: float,
L0189:     ) -> bool:
L0190:         """
L0191:         ✅ Step 3 신규: BEAR_REVERSAL 조건 체크
L0192:         RSI≤28 + Fear&Greed≤20 + BB%≤0.05 중 2개 이상
L0193:         + 하락 추세 조건 (ADX>20 이고 DI- > DI+)
L0194:         """
L0195:         is_downtrend = (adx > 20 and di_minus > di_plus) or (di_minus > di_plus * 1.3)
L0196:         if not is_downtrend:
L0197:             return False
L0198:         reversal_signals = 0
L0199:         if rsi <= 28:
L0200:             reversal_signals += 1
L0201:         if fear_greed_index is not None and fear_greed_index <= 20:
L0202:             reversal_signals += 1
L0203:         if bb_pct <= 0.05:
L0204:             reversal_signals += 1
L0205:         return reversal_signals >= 2
L0206:     def _classify(
L0207:         self,
L0208:         adx: float, di_plus: float, di_minus: float,
L0209:         bb_width: float, atr_pct: float, historical_vol: float,
L0210:         hurst: float, ema_bull_aligned: bool, ema_bear_aligned: bool,
L0211:         price: float, ema200: float,
L0212:     ) -> MarketRegime:
L0213:         """레짐 분류 결정 트리"""
L0214:         if atr_pct > 5.0 or historical_vol > 100:
L0215:             return MarketRegime.VOLATILE
L0216:         if adx > self.adx_trend_threshold and hurst > 0.55:
L0217:             if di_plus > di_minus and ema_bull_aligned:
L0218:                 return MarketRegime.TRENDING_UP
L0219:             elif di_minus > di_plus and ema_bear_aligned:
L0220:                 return MarketRegime.TRENDING_DOWN
L0221:             elif di_plus > di_minus and price > ema200:
L0222:                 return MarketRegime.TRENDING_UP
L0223:             else:
L0224:                 return MarketRegime.TRENDING_DOWN
L0225:         if adx < self.adx_trend_threshold and (
L0226:             bb_width < self.bb_squeeze_threshold or hurst < 0.45
L0227:         ):
L0228:             return MarketRegime.RANGING
L0229:         if atr_pct > self.vol_threshold * 2:
L0230:             return MarketRegime.VOLATILE
L0231:         return MarketRegime.TRENDING_UP if price > ema200 else MarketRegime.TRENDING_DOWN
L0232:     @staticmethod
L0233:     def _calc_hurst(series: pd.Series, lags: range = None) -> float:
L0234:         """
L0235:         ✅ Step 3 수정: 허스트 지수 계산 안정화
L0236:         log(0) 방지 + 최소 데이터 수 체크 강화
L0237:         """
L0238:         if len(series) < 20:
L0239:             return 0.5
L0240:         lags        = lags or range(2, min(20, len(series) // 2))
L0241:         log_returns = np.log(
L0242:             series.clip(lower=1e-10) / series.shift(1).clip(lower=1e-10)
L0243:         ).dropna().values
L0244:         if len(log_returns) < 10:
L0245:             return 0.5
L0246:         rs_values = []
L0247:         for lag in lags:
L0248:             chunks = [
L0249:                 log_returns[i:i+lag]
L0250:                 for i in range(0, len(log_returns) - lag + 1, lag)
L0251:             ]
L0252:             rs_list = []
L0253:             for c in chunks:
L0254:                 if len(c) != lag:
L0255:                     continue
L0256:                 std_c = np.std(c)
L0257:                 if std_c < 1e-10:
L0258:                     continue
L0259:                 cum   = np.cumsum(c - c.mean())
L0260:                 r_s   = (cum.max() - cum.min()) / std_c
L0261:                 if r_s > 0:
L0262:                     rs_list.append(r_s)
L0263:             if rs_list:
L0264:                 rs_values.append(np.mean(rs_list))
L0265:         if len(rs_values) < 2:
L0266:             return 0.5
L0267:         try:
L0268:             log_lags = np.log(list(lags)[:len(rs_values)])
L0269:             log_rs   = np.log(np.array(rs_values) + 1e-10)
L0270:             hurst    = np.polyfit(log_lags, log_rs, 1)[0]
L0271:             return float(np.clip(hurst, 0.0, 1.0))
L0272:         except Exception:
L0273:             return 0.5
L0274:     def get_allowed_strategies(self, regime: MarketRegime) -> Optional[List[str]]:
L0275:         """레짐별 허용 전략 목록 (None = 모두 허용)"""
L0276:         return REGIME_ALLOWED_STRATEGIES.get(regime.value, None)
L0277:     def get_regime_strategy_preference(self, regime: MarketRegime) -> Dict:
L0278:         """레짐별 전략 선호도 반환 (하위 호환)"""
L0279:         allowed = self.get_allowed_strategies(regime)
L0280:         preferences = {
L0281:             MarketRegime.TRENDING_UP: {
L0282:                 "preferred":   ["MACD_Cross", "Supertrend", "OrderBlock_SMC"],
L0283:                 "avoid":       ["VWAP_Reversion", "Bollinger_Squeeze"],
L0284:                 "description": "모멘텀 전략 선호",
L0285:             },
L0286:             MarketRegime.TRENDING_DOWN: {
L0287:                 "preferred":   [],
L0288:                 "avoid":       ["RSI_Divergence"],
L0289:                 "description": "하락 추세 — 신규 매수 차단 (BEAR_REVERSAL 예외)",
L0290:             },
L0291:             MarketRegime.RANGING: {
L0292:                 "preferred":   ["VWAP_Reversion", "Bollinger_Squeeze", "RSI_Divergence"],
L0293:                 "avoid":       ["MACD_Cross", "Supertrend"],
L0294:                 "description": "평균회귀 전략 선호",
L0295:             },
L0296:             MarketRegime.VOLATILE: {
L0297:                 "preferred":   ["VolBreakout", "ATR_Channel"],
L0298:                 "avoid":       ["VWAP_Reversion"],
L0299:                 "description": "변동성 전략 + 포지션 축소",
L0300:             },
L0301:             MarketRegime.BEAR_REVERSAL: {
L0302:                 "preferred":   ["RSI_Divergence", "VWAP_Reversion", "Bollinger_Squeeze"],
L0303:                 "avoid":       ["MACD_Cross", "Supertrend", "VolBreakout"],
L0304:                 "description": "역발상 매수 — 포지션 50% 축소, 임계값 -1.5 하향",
L0305:             },
L0306:         }
L0307:         return preferences.get(regime, {
L0308:             "preferred": [], "avoid": [], "description": "레짐 불명"
L0309:         })
L0310:     def get_cached_regime(self, market: str) -> MarketRegime:
L0311:         return self._cache.get(market, MarketRegime.UNKNOWN)
L0312:     def is_tradeable(self, regime: MarketRegime) -> bool:
L0313:         """해당 레짐에서 매수 가능 여부"""
L0314:         allowed = self.get_allowed_strategies(regime)
L0315:         return allowed is None or len(allowed) > 0

FILE: signals/filters/trend_filter.py  (5.4KB → 4.9KB)

L0001: """
L0002: Layer 2 트렌드 필터:
L0003:   1) 일봉 EMA(200) 위: 강세장 → 매수 허용
L0004:   2) 일봉 EMA(200) 아래: 약세장 → 매수 차단 (BEAR_REVERSAL만 허용)
L0005:   3) 4시간봉 EMA(50) 방향 → 중기 트렌드 확인
L0006:   4) 시장 레짐 판단: TRENDING / RANGING / VOLATILE
L0007: """
L0008: import numpy as np
L0009: import pandas as pd
L0010: from typing import Optional
L0011: from utils.logger import logger
L0012: class TrendFilter:
L0013:     EMA200_PERIOD = 200
L0014:     EMA50_PERIOD  = 50
L0015:     EMA20_PERIOD  = 20
L0016:     ADX_PERIOD    = 14
L0017:     ADX_TRENDING  = 25
L0018:     ADX_VOLATILE  = 40
L0019:     def is_buy_allowed(
L0020:         self,
L0021:         daily_df: pd.DataFrame,
L0022:         h4_df: Optional[pd.DataFrame] = None,
L0023:         strategy: str = "default",
L0024:     ) -> dict:
L0025:         """
L0026:         매수 허용 여부 + 트렌드 정보 반환
L0027:         Returns: {
L0028:             "allowed": bool,
L0029:             "regime":  "BULL" | "BEAR" | "NEUTRAL",
L0030:             "ema200":  float,
L0031:             "reason":  str,
L0032:         }
L0033:         """
L0034:         result = self._check_daily(daily_df)
L0035:         if not result["allowed"] and strategy == "BEAR_REVERSAL":
L0036:             result["allowed"] = True
L0037:             result["reason"]  += " (BEAR_REVERSAL 예외)"
L0038:         if result["allowed"] and h4_df is not None:
L0039:             h4_check = self._check_h4(h4_df)
L0040:             if not h4_check["trending"]:
L0041:                 result["reason"] += f" | 4H:{h4_check['reason']}"
L0042:         return result
L0043:     def get_regime(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> str:
L0044:         """
L0045:         시장 레짐 감지
L0046:         Returns: "TRENDING_UP" | "TRENDING_DOWN" | "RANGING" | "VOLATILE"
L0047:         """
L0048:         if len(df) < self.ADX_PERIOD + 5:
L0049:             return "RANGING"
L0050:         adx   = self._calc_adx(df)
L0051:         close = df["close"].iloc[-1]
L0052:         ema20 = self._ema(df["close"], self.EMA20_PERIOD).iloc[-1]
L0053:         if adx > self.ADX_VOLATILE:
L0054:             return "VOLATILE"
L0055:         elif adx > self.ADX_TRENDING:
L0056:             return "TRENDING_UP" if close > ema20 else "TRENDING_DOWN"
L0057:         else:
L0058:             return "RANGING"
L0059:     def _check_daily(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> dict:
L0060:         if len(df) < self.EMA200_PERIOD:
L0061:             return {
L0062:                 "allowed": True,
L0063:                 "regime":  "NEUTRAL",
L0064:                 "ema200":  0.0,
L0065:                 "reason":  "일봉 데이터 부족 → 매수 허용",
L0066:             }
L0067:         close  = df["close"].iloc[-1]
L0068:         ema200 = self._ema(df["close"], self.EMA200_PERIOD).iloc[-1]
L0069:         diff_pct = (close - ema200) / ema200 * 100
L0070:         if close > ema200:
L0071:             return {
L0072:                 "allowed": True,
L0073:                 "regime":  "BULL",
L0074:                 "ema200":  ema200,
L0075:                 "reason":  f"일봉 EMA200 위 (+{diff_pct:.1f}%) → 매수 허용",
L0076:             }
L0077:         elif diff_pct > -35.0:
L0078:             return {
L0079:                 "allowed": True,
L0080:                 "regime":  "BEAR",
L0081:                 "ema200":  ema200,
L0082:                 "reason":  f"일봉 EMA200 하회({diff_pct:.1f}%) → BEAR 완화 허용",
L0083:             }
L0084:         else:
L0085:             return {
L0086:                 "allowed": False,
L0087:                 "regime":  "BEAR",
L0088:                 "ema200":  ema200,
L0089:                 "reason":  f"일봉 EMA200 하회({diff_pct:.1f}%) → 매수 차단 (과도 하락)",
L0090:             }
L0091:     def _check_h4(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> dict:
L0092:         if len(df) < self.EMA50_PERIOD:
L0093:             return {"trending": True, "reason": "4H 데이터 부족"}
L0094:         close = df["close"].iloc[-1]
L0095:         ema50 = self._ema(df["close"], self.EMA50_PERIOD).iloc[-1]
L0096:         trending = close > ema50 * 0.98
L0097:         return {
L0098:             "trending": trending,
L0099:             "reason":   f"4H EMA50={'위' if trending else '아래'}",
L0100:         }
L0101:     @staticmethod
L0102:     def _ema(series: pd.Series, period: int) -> pd.Series:
L0103:         return series.ewm(span=period, adjust=False).mean()
L0104:     def _calc_adx(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> float:
L0105:         high  = df["high"].values
L0106:         low   = df["low"].values
L0107:         close = df["close"].values
L0108:         n     = self.ADX_PERIOD
L0109:         if len(df) < n * 2:
L0110:             return 20.0
L0111:         tr_list, pdm_list, ndm_list = [], [], []
L0112:         for i in range(1, len(df)):
L0113:             tr  = max(high[i]-low[i], abs(high[i]-close[i-1]), abs(low[i]-close[i-1]))
L0114:             pdm = max(high[i]-high[i-1], 0)
L0115:             ndm = max(low[i-1]-low[i],   0)
L0116:             if pdm < ndm: pdm = 0
L0117:             elif ndm < pdm: ndm = 0
L0118:             tr_list.append(tr); pdm_list.append(pdm); ndm_list.append(ndm)
L0119:         atr  = self._wilder_smooth(tr_list,  n)
L0120:         pdi  = 100 * self._wilder_smooth(pdm_list, n) / (atr + 1e-9)
L0121:         ndi  = 100 * self._wilder_smooth(ndm_list, n) / (atr + 1e-9)
L0122:         dx   = 100 * abs(pdi - ndi) / (pdi + ndi + 1e-9)
L0123:         return float(dx)
L0124:     @staticmethod
L0125:     def _wilder_smooth(data: list, n: int) -> float:
L0126:         if len(data) < n:
L0127:             return float(np.mean(data)) if data else 0.0
L0128:         val = sum(data[:n])
L0129:         for d in data[n:]:
L0130:             val = val - val / n + d
L0131:         return val

FILE: signals/filters/volume_profile.py  (5.6KB → 4.7KB)

L0001: """
L0002: APEX BOT - 거래량 프로파일 분석
L0003: POC(Point of Control), HVN/LVN, Value Area 계산
L0004: """
L0005: import numpy as np
L0006: import pandas as pd
L0007: from typing import Dict, Optional, Tuple
L0008: from dataclasses import dataclass
L0009: from loguru import logger
L0010: @dataclass
L0011: class VolumeProfileResult:
L0012:     poc_price: float
L0013:     vah: float
L0014:     val: float
L0015:     above_poc: bool
L0016:     hvn_levels: list
L0017:     lvn_levels: list
L0018: class VolumeProfileAnalyzer:
L0019:     """
L0020:     거래량 프로파일 분석
L0021:     - POC: 가장 많이 거래된 가격대 (강한 지지/저항)
L0022:     - Value Area: 전체 거래량의 70% 집중 구간
L0023:     - HVN: 거래량 밀집 구간 (저항/지지 강함)
L0024:     - LVN: 거래량 희박 구간 (가격 빠르게 통과)
L0025:     """
L0026:     def __init__(self, bins: int = 50, value_area_pct: float = 0.70):
L0027:         self.bins = bins
L0028:         self.value_area_pct = value_area_pct
L0029:     def analyze(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> Optional[VolumeProfileResult]:
L0030:         """거래량 프로파일 계산"""
L0031:         try:
L0032:             if len(df) < 20:
L0033:                 return None
L0034:             high = df["high"].values
L0035:             low = df["low"].values
L0036:             volume = df["volume"].values
L0037:             close = df["close"].values
L0038:             price_min = low.min()
L0039:             price_max = high.max()
L0040:             price_range = np.linspace(price_min, price_max, self.bins + 1)
L0041:             vol_profile = np.zeros(self.bins)
L0042:             for i in range(len(df)):
L0043:                 candle_low = low[i]
L0044:                 candle_high = high[i]
L0045:                 candle_vol = volume[i]
L0046:                 for j in range(self.bins):
L0047:                     bin_low = price_range[j]
L0048:                     bin_high = price_range[j + 1]
L0049:                     overlap_low = max(candle_low, bin_low)
L0050:                     overlap_high = min(candle_high, bin_high)
L0051:                     if overlap_high > overlap_low:
L0052:                         candle_range = candle_high - candle_low + 1e-8
L0053:                         overlap_ratio = (overlap_high - overlap_low) / candle_range
L0054:                         vol_profile[j] += candle_vol * overlap_ratio
L0055:             poc_idx = np.argmax(vol_profile)
L0056:             poc_price = (price_range[poc_idx] + price_range[poc_idx + 1]) / 2
L0057:             total_vol = vol_profile.sum()
L0058:             target_vol = total_vol * self.value_area_pct
L0059:             va_low_idx = poc_idx
L0060:             va_high_idx = poc_idx
L0061:             accumulated = vol_profile[poc_idx]
L0062:             while accumulated < target_vol:
L0063:                 expand_up = va_high_idx < self.bins - 1
L0064:                 expand_down = va_low_idx > 0
L0065:                 if not expand_up and not expand_down:
L0066:                     break
L0067:                 up_vol = vol_profile[va_high_idx + 1] if expand_up else 0
L0068:                 down_vol = vol_profile[va_low_idx - 1] if expand_down else 0
L0069:                 if up_vol >= down_vol and expand_up:
L0070:                     va_high_idx += 1
L0071:                     accumulated += up_vol
L0072:                 elif expand_down:
L0073:                     va_low_idx -= 1
L0074:                     accumulated += down_vol
L0075:                 else:
L0076:                     break
L0077:             vah = (price_range[va_high_idx] + price_range[va_high_idx + 1]) / 2
L0078:             val = (price_range[va_low_idx] + price_range[va_low_idx + 1]) / 2
L0079:             avg_vol = np.mean(vol_profile)
L0080:             hvn_levels = []
L0081:             lvn_levels = []
L0082:             for j in range(self.bins):
L0083:                 mid_price = (price_range[j] + price_range[j + 1]) / 2
L0084:                 if vol_profile[j] > avg_vol * 1.5:
L0085:                     hvn_levels.append(mid_price)
L0086:                 elif vol_profile[j] < avg_vol * 0.5:
L0087:                     lvn_levels.append(mid_price)
L0088:             current_price = close[-1]
L0089:             return VolumeProfileResult(
L0090:                 poc_price=poc_price,
L0091:                 vah=vah,
L0092:                 val=val,
L0093:                 above_poc=current_price > poc_price,
L0094:                 hvn_levels=hvn_levels,
L0095:                 lvn_levels=lvn_levels
L0096:             )
L0097:         except Exception as e:
L0098:             logger.debug(f"거래량 프로파일 오류: {e}")
L0099:             return None
L0100:     def get_nearest_support_resistance(self, df: pd.DataFrame, current_price: float) -> Dict:
L0101:         """현재가 기준 가장 가까운 지지/저항 반환"""
L0102:         result = self.analyze(df)
L0103:         if not result:
L0104:             return {}
L0105:         support = max([p for p in result.hvn_levels if p < current_price], default=result.val)
L0106:         resistance = min([p for p in result.hvn_levels if p > current_price], default=result.vah)
L0107:         return {
L0108:             "poc": result.poc_price,
L0109:             "support": support,
L0110:             "resistance": resistance,
L0111:             "vah": result.vah,
L0112:             "val": result.val,
L0113:             "above_poc": result.above_poc,
L0114:             "risk_reward": (resistance - current_price) / (current_price - support + 1e-8)
L0115:         }

FILE: signals/filters/correlation_filter.py  (11.3KB → 9.1KB)

L0001: """
L0002: APEX BOT - 상관관계 필터 (Correlation Filter)
L0003: BTC 급락 시 알트코인 동시 손절 방지
L0004: - BTC 가격 변화율이 임계치 초과 시 알트코인 신규 매수 차단
L0005: - 상관관계 높은 코인 동시 포지션 제한
L0006: - 시장 충격(Market Shock) 감지
L0007: """
L0008: from __future__ import annotations
L0009: import time
L0010: from collections import deque
L0011: from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
L0012: import numpy as np
L0013: from loguru import logger
L0014: class CorrelationFilter:
L0015:     """
L0016:     BTC 기반 상관관계 리스크 필터
L0017:     주요 기능:
L0018:     1. BTC 단기 급락 감지 → 알트 매수 차단
L0019:     2. 포트폴리오 상관관계 계산 → 동시 포지션 제한
L0020:     3. 시장 충격 감지 (Market Shock Detection)
L0021:     4. 변동성 스파이크 감지
L0022:     사용법:
L0023:         cf = CorrelationFilter()
L0024:         cf.update_price("KRW-BTC", btc_price)
L0025:         ok, reason = cf.can_buy("KRW-ETH", open_positions)
L0026:         if not ok:
L0027:             logger.warning(f"상관관계 필터 차단: {reason}")
L0028:     """
L0029:     BTC_MARKET = "KRW-BTC"
L0030:     BTC_SHOCK_5MIN  = -0.025
L0031:     BTC_SHOCK_1H    = -0.050
L0032:     BTC_SPIKE_5MIN  = +0.030
L0033:     VOL_SPIKE_MULT  = 2.5
L0034:     BLOCK_DURATION_SHOCK = 30 * 60
L0035:     BLOCK_DURATION_SEVERE = 120 * 60
L0036:     def __init__(self,
L0037:                  btc_shock_threshold: float = BTC_SHOCK_5MIN,
L0038:                  block_duration: int = BLOCK_DURATION_SHOCK):
L0039:         self._btc_shock_threshold = btc_shock_threshold
L0040:         self._block_duration = block_duration
L0041:         self._price_history: Dict[str, deque] = {}
L0042:         self._blocked_until: Dict[str, float] = {}
L0043:         self._global_block_until: float = 0.0
L0044:         self._block_reason: str = ""
L0045:         self._volatility: Dict[str, deque] = {}
L0046:         logger.info("✅ 상관관계 필터 초기화")
L0047:     def update_price(self, market: str, price: float):
L0048:         """가격 업데이트 (엔진에서 매 tick 호출)"""
L0049:         if market not in self._price_history:
L0050:             self._price_history[market] = deque(maxlen=360)
L0051:         self._price_history[market].append((time.time(), price))
L0052:         self._volatility.setdefault(market, deque(maxlen=60))
L0053:         if market == self.BTC_MARKET:
L0054:             self._check_btc_shock()
L0055:     def update_prices(self, price_map: Dict[str, float]):
L0056:         """다중 마켓 가격 일괄 업데이트"""
L0057:         for market, price in price_map.items():
L0058:             self.update_price(market, price)
L0059:     def can_buy(
L0060:         self,
L0061:         market: str,
L0062:         open_positions: List[str] = None,
L0063:     ) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
L0064:         """
L0065:         매수 가능 여부 확인
L0066:         Returns:
L0067:             (가능 여부, 사유)
L0068:         """
L0069:         now = time.time()
L0070:         if now < self._global_block_until:
L0071:             remaining = int(self._global_block_until - now)
L0072:             return False, f"BTC 충격 차단 ({remaining//60}분 {remaining%60}초): {self._block_reason}"
L0073:         blocked = self._blocked_until.get(market, 0)
L0074:         if now < blocked:
L0075:             remaining = int(blocked - now)
L0076:             return False, f"{market} 개별 차단 ({remaining//60}분 {remaining%60}초)"
L0077:         btc_trend_ok, btc_msg = self._check_btc_trend()
L0078:         if not btc_trend_ok:
L0079:             return False, btc_msg
L0080:         if self._is_volatility_spike(market):
L0081:             return False, f"{market} 변동성 스파이크 감지 → 매수 대기"
L0082:         if open_positions:
L0083:             corr_ok, corr_msg = self._check_portfolio_correlation(
L0084:                 market, open_positions
L0085:             )
L0086:             if not corr_ok:
L0087:                 return False, corr_msg
L0088:         return True, "OK"
L0089:     def can_maintain_position(self, market: str) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
L0090:         """
L0091:         기존 포지션 유지 여부 (비상 청산 권고)
L0092:         Returns:
L0093:             (유지 권장, 사유)
L0094:         """
L0095:         if market == self.BTC_MARKET:
L0096:             return True, "BTC는 직접 청산 판단"
L0097:         btc_ret_1h = self._get_return(self.BTC_MARKET, window_seconds=3600)
L0098:         if btc_ret_1h is not None and btc_ret_1h < self.BTC_SHOCK_1H:
L0099:             return False, (
L0100:                 f"BTC 1시간 급락 {btc_ret_1h:.2%} → {market} 청산 권고"
L0101:             )
L0102:         return True, "OK"
L0103:     def _check_btc_shock(self):
L0104:         """BTC 급락/급등 감지 → 글로벌 차단 설정"""
L0105:         ret_5m  = self._get_return(self.BTC_MARKET, window_seconds=300)
L0106:         ret_15m = self._get_return(self.BTC_MARKET, window_seconds=900)
L0107:         ret_1h  = self._get_return(self.BTC_MARKET, window_seconds=3600)
L0108:         now = time.time()
L0109:         if ret_1h is not None and ret_1h < self.BTC_SHOCK_1H:
L0110:             self._global_block_until = now + self.BLOCK_DURATION_SEVERE
L0111:             self._block_reason = f"BTC 1h 급락 {ret_1h:.2%}"
L0112:             logger.warning(
L0113:                 f"🚨 BTC 심각 급락 감지: {ret_1h:.2%} (1h) → "
L0114:                 f"전체 매수 {self.BLOCK_DURATION_SEVERE//60}분 차단"
L0115:             )
L0116:             return
L0117:         if ret_5m is not None and ret_5m < self._btc_shock_threshold:
L0118:             self._global_block_until = now + self._block_duration
L0119:             self._block_reason = f"BTC 5m 급락 {ret_5m:.2%}"
L0120:             logger.warning(
L0121:                 f"⚠️ BTC 급락 감지: {ret_5m:.2%} (5m) → "
L0122:                 f"전체 매수 {self._block_duration//60}분 차단"
L0123:             )
L0124:             return
L0125:         if ret_15m is not None and ret_15m < -0.03:
L0126:             self._global_block_until = now + self._block_duration
L0127:             self._block_reason = f"BTC 15m 하락 {ret_15m:.2%}"
L0128:             logger.warning(
L0129:                 f"⚠️ BTC 15분 하락: {ret_15m:.2%} → 매수 차단"
L0130:             )
L0131:     def _check_btc_trend(self) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
L0132:         """BTC 단기 추세 확인 (매수 판단 시 호출)"""
L0133:         ret_5m = self._get_return(self.BTC_MARKET, window_seconds=300)
L0134:         if ret_5m is None:
L0135:             return True, "OK"
L0136:         if ret_5m < self._btc_shock_threshold * 0.7:
L0137:             return False, f"BTC 5분 하락 중 ({ret_5m:.2%}) → 매수 대기"
L0138:         return True, "OK"
L0139:     def _is_volatility_spike(self, market: str) -> bool:
L0140:         """변동성 스파이크 감지"""
L0141:         history = self._price_history.get(market)
L0142:         if not history or len(history) < 20:
L0143:             return False
L0144:         prices = np.array([p for _, p in history])
L0145:         returns = np.diff(prices) / prices[:-1]
L0146:         if len(returns) < 10:
L0147:             return False
L0148:         recent_vol = abs(returns[-1])
L0149:         avg_vol = np.std(returns[:-1])
L0150:         if avg_vol > 0 and recent_vol > avg_vol * self.VOL_SPIKE_MULT:
L0151:             logger.debug(
L0152:                 f"⚡ 변동성 스파이크: {market} | "
L0153:                 f"현재={recent_vol:.4f} > 평균={avg_vol:.4f} × {self.VOL_SPIKE_MULT}"
L0154:             )
L0155:             return True
L0156:         return False
L0157:     def _check_portfolio_correlation(
L0158:         self,
L0159:         market: str,
L0160:         open_positions: List[str],
L0161:     ) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
L0162:         """
L0163:         포트폴리오 내 상관관계 확인
L0164:         BTC, ETH 등 고상관 코인 동시 3개 이상 보유 제한
L0165:         """
L0166:         HIGH_CORR_GROUP = {
L0167:             "KRW-BTC", "KRW-ETH", "KRW-BNB", "KRW-SOL",
L0168:             "KRW-ADA", "KRW-DOT", "KRW-AVAX", "KRW-ATOM",
L0169:         }
L0170:         corr_count = sum(
L0171:             1 for pos in open_positions if pos in HIGH_CORR_GROUP
L0172:         )
L0173:         if market in HIGH_CORR_GROUP and corr_count >= 6:
L0174:             return (
L0175:                 False,
L0176:                 f"고상관 포지션 한도 초과 ({corr_count}/3): "
L0177:                 f"{', '.join(p for p in open_positions if p in HIGH_CORR_GROUP)}"
L0178:             )
L0179:         return True, "OK"
L0180:     def _get_return(self, market: str, window_seconds: int) -> Optional[float]:
L0181:         """
L0182:         특정 시간 창 내 수익률 계산
L0183:         Args:
L0184:             window_seconds: 기간 (초)
L0185:         Returns:
L0186:             수익률 (None = 데이터 부족)
L0187:         """
L0188:         history = self._price_history.get(market)
L0189:         if not history or len(history) < 2:
L0190:             return None
L0191:         now = time.time()
L0192:         cutoff = now - window_seconds
L0193:         start_price = None
L0194:         for ts, price in history:
L0195:             if ts >= cutoff:
L0196:                 start_price = price
L0197:                 break
L0198:         if start_price is None or start_price == 0:
L0199:             return None
L0200:         current_price = history[-1][1]
L0201:         return (current_price - start_price) / start_price
L0202:     def get_btc_status(self) -> Dict:
L0203:         """BTC 현재 상태 요약"""
L0204:         ret_5m  = self._get_return(self.BTC_MARKET, 300)
L0205:         ret_15m = self._get_return(self.BTC_MARKET, 900)
L0206:         ret_1h  = self._get_return(self.BTC_MARKET, 3600)
L0207:         now = time.time()
L0208:         is_blocked = now < self._global_block_until
L0209:         remaining = max(0, int(self._global_block_until - now))
L0210:         return {
L0211:             "is_globally_blocked": is_blocked,
L0212:             "block_remaining_sec": remaining,
L0213:             "block_reason": self._block_reason if is_blocked else "",
L0214:             "btc_ret_5m":  ret_5m,
L0215:             "btc_ret_15m": ret_15m,
L0216:             "btc_ret_1h":  ret_1h,
L0217:         }
L0218:     def force_unblock(self):
L0219:         """수동 차단 해제 (관리자용)"""
L0220:         self._global_block_until = 0
L0221:         self._blocked_until.clear()
L0222:         self._block_reason = ""
L0223:         logger.info("✅ 상관관계 필터 차단 수동 해제")

FILE: signals/filters/volume_spike.py  (6.1KB → 5.4KB)

L0001: """
L0002: APEX BOT - 거래량 스파이크 감지 (Volume Spike Detector)
L0003: 이상 거래량 발생 전후 신호 포착 → 선행 진입 or 이탈 경고
L0004: 감지 로직:
L0005:   1. 거래량이 20봉 평균 대비 N배 초과 → 스파이크 감지
L0006:   2. 스파이크 + 가격 상승 → 강한 매수 신호 보정
L0007:   3. 스파이크 + 가격 하락 → 덤핑 경고 (매수 차단)
L0008:   4. 연속 스파이크 (2봉 이상) → 추세 전환 신호
L0009: """
L0010: from __future__ import annotations
L0011: from dataclasses import dataclass
L0012: from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
L0013: import numpy as np
L0014: import pandas as pd
L0015: from loguru import logger
L0016: @dataclass
L0017: class VolumeSpike:
L0018:     """감지된 거래량 스파이크"""
L0019:     market: str
L0020:     ratio: float
L0021:     direction: str
L0022:     price_change: float
L0023:     strength: float
L0024: class VolumeSpikeDetector:
L0025:     """
L0026:     거래량 스파이크 감지 및 신호 보정기
L0027:     사용법:
L0028:         vsd = VolumeSpikeDetector()
L0029:         spike = vsd.detect(df, market)
L0030:         if spike:
L0031:             adj = vsd.get_confidence_adjustment(spike)
L0032:             signal.confidence += adj
L0033:     """
L0034:     SPIKE_THRESHOLD  = 2.0
L0035:     STRONG_THRESHOLD = 3.5
L0036:     EXTREME_THRESHOLD = 6.0
L0037:     MA_PERIOD = 20
L0038:     def __init__(self,
L0039:                  spike_threshold: float = SPIKE_THRESHOLD,
L0040:                  ma_period: int = MA_PERIOD):
L0041:         self._threshold = spike_threshold
L0042:         self._ma_period = ma_period
L0043:         self._spike_history: Dict[str, List[VolumeSpike]] = {}
L0044:     def detect(
L0045:         self,
L0046:         df: pd.DataFrame,
L0047:         market: str,
L0048:         lookback: int = 3,
L0049:     ) -> Optional[VolumeSpike]:
L0050:         """
L0051:         DataFrame에서 최근 N봉 스파이크 감지
L0052:         Args:
L0053:             df:       OHLCV DataFrame (volume 컬럼 필요)
L0054:             market:   마켓 코드
L0055:             lookback: 최근 N봉 스캔
L0056:         Returns:
L0057:             VolumeSpike 또는 None
L0058:         """
L0059:         if df is None or len(df) < self._ma_period + lookback:
L0060:             return None
L0061:         if "volume" not in df.columns:
L0062:             return None
L0063:         vol = df["volume"].values
L0064:         close = df["close"].values
L0065:         ma_vol = vol[-(self._ma_period + lookback):-lookback].mean()
L0066:         if ma_vol <= 0:
L0067:             return None
L0068:         for i in range(lookback, 0, -1):
L0069:             current_vol = vol[-i]
L0070:             ratio = current_vol / ma_vol
L0071:             if ratio >= self._threshold:
L0072:                 if len(close) > i:
L0073:                     price_change = (close[-i] - close[-i-1]) / close[-i-1]
L0074:                 else:
L0075:                     price_change = 0.0
L0076:                 if price_change > 0.005:
L0077:                     direction = "UP"
L0078:                 elif price_change < -0.005:
L0079:                     direction = "DOWN"
L0080:                 else:
L0081:                     direction = "NEUTRAL"
L0082:                 strength = min((ratio - self._threshold) / (self.EXTREME_THRESHOLD - self._threshold), 1.0)
L0083:                 spike = VolumeSpike(
L0084:                     market=market,
L0085:                     ratio=ratio,
L0086:                     direction=direction,
L0087:                     price_change=price_change,
L0088:                     strength=strength,
L0089:                 )
L0090:                 self._spike_history.setdefault(market, [])
L0091:                 self._spike_history[market].append(spike)
L0092:                 if len(self._spike_history[market]) > 10:
L0093:                     self._spike_history[market] = self._spike_history[market][-10:]
L0094:                 logger.debug(
L0095:                     f"⚡ 거래량 스파이크 | {market} | "
L0096:                     f"비율={ratio:.1f}x | 방향={direction} | "
L0097:                     f"가격변화={price_change:.2%}"
L0098:                 )
L0099:                 return spike
L0100:         return None
L0101:     def get_confidence_adjustment(self, spike: Optional[VolumeSpike]) -> float:
L0102:         """
L0103:         스파이크 기반 신뢰도 보정값 반환
L0104:         Returns:
L0105:             -0.20 ~ +0.20 범위
L0106:         """
L0107:         if spike is None:
L0108:             return 0.0
L0109:         base = spike.strength * 0.15
L0110:         if spike.direction == "UP":
L0111:             return base
L0112:         elif spike.direction == "DOWN":
L0113:             return -base * 1.5
L0114:         else:
L0115:             return base * 0.3
L0116:     def is_dumping(self, df: pd.DataFrame, market: str) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
L0117:         """
L0118:         덤핑(대량 매도) 감지
L0119:         Returns:
L0120:             (덤핑 여부, 사유)
L0121:         """
L0122:         spike = self.detect(df, market, lookback=2)
L0123:         if spike and spike.direction == "DOWN":
L0124:             if spike.ratio >= self.STRONG_THRESHOLD:
L0125:                 return (
L0126:                     True,
L0127:                     f"{market} 대량 매도 감지 ({spike.ratio:.1f}x, {spike.price_change:.2%})"
L0128:                 )
L0129:         return False, "OK"
L0130:     def is_breakout(self, df: pd.DataFrame, market: str) -> Tuple[bool, float]:
L0131:         """
L0132:         거래량 돌파 감지 (매수 신호 보강)
L0133:         Returns:
L0134:             (돌파 여부, 신뢰도 보정값)
L0135:         """
L0136:         spike = self.detect(df, market, lookback=2)
L0137:         if spike and spike.direction == "UP":
L0138:             adj = self.get_confidence_adjustment(spike)
L0139:             return True, adj
L0140:         return False, 0.0
L0141:     def get_volume_ratio(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> float:
L0142:         """현재 거래량 / 평균 거래량 비율"""
L0143:         if df is None or len(df) < self._ma_period + 1:
L0144:             return 1.0
L0145:         vol = df["volume"].values
L0146:         ma = vol[-(self._ma_period+1):-1].mean()
L0147:         if ma <= 0:
L0148:             return 1.0
L0149:         return vol[-1] / ma
L0150:     def get_spike_history(self, market: str) -> List[VolumeSpike]:
L0151:         return self._spike_history.get(market, [])

L0151:         """뉴스 수집 (캐시 유효 시 스킵)"""

L0170:     def get_signal_boost(self, market: str) -> Tuple[float, float]:

L0182:         boost = max(-2.0, min(2.0, boost))
L0183:         return round(combined, 3), round(boost, 3)

L0287:                                 source="coindesk")

L0293:     def _score_item(self, item: NewsItem):
L0294:         """단일 뉴스 아이템 감성 점수 계산"""

L0298:                 result = self._finbert(item.title[:512])[0]

L0301:                 if label == "positive":

L0303:                 elif label == "negative":
L0304:                     item.sentiment_score = -conf
L0305:                 else:
L0306:                     item.sentiment_score = 0.0

L0309:                 pass

L0313:                 item.sentiment_score = vs["compound"]
L0314:                 item.sentiment_score = self._apply_keywords(
L0315:                     title_lower, item.sentiment_score
L0316:                 )
L0317:                 return
L0318:             except Exception:
L0319:                 pass

L0321:     def _keyword_score(self, text: str) -> float:
L0322:         """키워드 기반 점수 계산"""
L0323:         score = 0.0
L0324:         hits = 0
L0325:         for kw, val in BULLISH_KEYWORDS.items():
L0326:             if kw in text:
L0327:                 score += val
L0328:                 hits += 1
L0329:         for kw, val in BEARISH_KEYWORDS.items():
L0330:             if kw in text:
L0331:                 score += val
L0332:                 hits += 1
L0333:         if hits == 0:
L0334:             return 0.0
L0335:         return max(-1.0, min(1.0, score / (hits * 4)))
L0336:     def _apply_keywords(self, text: str, base_score: float) -> float:
L0337:         """VADER 점수에 키워드 보정 적용"""
L0338:         kw_score = self._keyword_score(text)
L0339:         return base_score * 0.7 + kw_score * 0.3
L0340:     def _update_market_scores(self):
L0341:         """최근 1시간 뉴스로 마켓별 점수 업데이트"""
L0342:         cutoff = time.time() - 3600
L0343:         market_sums = defaultdict(list)
L0344:         global_sums = []
L0345:         for item in self._news_cache:
L0346:             if item.published_at < cutoff:
L0347:                 continue
L0348:             global_sums.append(item.sentiment_score)
L0349:             for market in item.coins:
L0350:                 market_sums[market].append(item.sentiment_score)
L0351:             title_lower = item.title.lower()
L0352:             for market, kws in COIN_KEYWORDS.items():
L0353:                 for kw in kws:
L0354:                     if kw in title_lower and market not in item.coins:
L0355:                         market_sums[market].append(item.sentiment_score)
L0356:         self._market_scores = defaultdict(float)
L0357:         if global_sums:
L0358:             self._market_scores["GLOBAL"] = sum(global_sums) / len(global_sums)
L0359:         for market, scores in market_sums.items():
L0360:             if scores:
L0361:                 self._market_scores[market] = sum(scores) / len(scores)
