L0001: """
L0002: APEX BOT - 호가창 신호 분석기 v2.0
L0003: 페이크월(가짜 지지/저항벽) 탐지 강화
L0004: ────────────────────────────────────
L0005: 개선 사항:
L0006:   1. 페이크월 탐지: 벽 크기가 평균의 3배 이상인 단일 레벨 감지
L0007:   2. 벽 소멸 감지: 히스토리 비교로 갑작스러운 벽 사라짐 = 페이크월
L0008:   3. 벽 출현 속도: 갑자기 3배 이상 증가한 벽 = 조작 가능성
L0009:   4. 근접 레벨 필터: 최우선호가 5단계 이내만 유효한 벽으로 인정
L0010: """
L0011: from __future__ import annotations
L0012: import time
L0013: from collections import deque
L0014: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
L0015: from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
L0016: import numpy as np
L0017: from loguru import logger
L0018: @dataclass
L0019: class OrderbookSignal:
L0020:     """호가창 분석 결과 (v2.0 — 페이크월 포함)"""
L0021:     market: str
L0022:     bid_ask_ratio: float
L0023:     spread_pct: float
L0024:     bid_wall_price: float
L0025:     ask_wall_price: float
L0026:     bid_concentration: float
L0027:     ask_concentration: float
L0028:     signal: str
L0029:     confidence: float
L0030:     reason: str
L0031:     fake_wall_detected: bool = False
L0032:     fake_wall_side: str = ""
L0033:     fake_wall_confidence: float = 0.0
L0034:     wall_vanished: bool = False
L0035:     wall_size_ratio: float = 0.0
L0036: class OrderbookSignalAnalyzer:
L0037:     """
L0038:     실시간 호가창 신호 분석기 v2.0
L0039:     ─────────────────────────────
L0040:     페이크월 판정 기준 (한국 시장 특화):
L0041:       1. 단일 레벨 크기 >= 평균 * WALL_THR (기본 3.0배)
L0042:       2. 최우선호가에서 5단계 이내 레벨만 유효
L0043:       3. 히스토리에서 1회만 등장 → 지속성 없음 → 페이크 가능성 높음
L0044:       4. 이전 스냅샷 대비 크기가 3배 이상 급증 → 조작 가능성
L0045:       5. 이전에 있던 벽이 30초 내 사라짐 → 페이크월 확정
L0046:     """
L0047:     BUY_PRESSURE_RATIO  = 1.5
L0048:     SELL_PRESSURE_RATIO = 1.5
L0049:     SPREAD_NORMAL_PCT   = 0.1
L0050:     SPREAD_WIDE_PCT     = 0.3
L0051:     TOP_N_LEVELS        = 5
L0052:     WALL_THR            = 3.0
L0053:     FAKE_WALL_VANISH_SEC = 30
L0054:     HISTORY_MAXLEN      = 8
L0055:     def __init__(self, wall_thr: float = 3.0, imbalance_thr: float = 0.3):
L0056:         self.WALL_THR = wall_thr
L0057:         self.imbalance_thr = imbalance_thr
L0058:         self._wall_history: Dict[str, deque] = {}
L0059:         self._last_snapshot: Dict[str, dict] = {}
L0060:     def analyze(
L0061:         self, market: str, orderbook: Dict
L0062:     ) -> Optional[OrderbookSignal]:
L0063:         if not orderbook:
L0064:             return None
L0065:         try:
L0066:             units = orderbook.get("orderbook_units", [])
L0067:             if not units:
L0068:                 return None
L0069:             bids = [
L0070:                 (float(u.get("bid_price", 0)), float(u.get("bid_size", 0)))
L0071:                 for u in units if u.get("bid_price", 0) > 0
L0072:             ]
L0073:             asks = [
L0074:                 (float(u.get("ask_price", 0)), float(u.get("ask_size", 0)))
L0075:                 for u in units if u.get("ask_price", 0) > 0
L0076:             ]
L0077:             if not bids or not asks:
L0078:                 return None
L0079:             best_bid   = bids[0][0]
L0080:             best_ask   = asks[0][0]
L0081:             spread     = (best_ask - best_bid) / best_ask * 100
L0082:             top_bids   = bids[:self.TOP_N_LEVELS]
L0083:             top_asks   = asks[:self.TOP_N_LEVELS]
L0084:             total_bids = sum(b[0] * b[1] for b in bids)
L0085:             total_asks = sum(a[0] * a[1] for a in asks)
L0086:             if total_bids < 1e-10 or total_asks < 1e-10:
L0087:                 return None
L0088:             top_bid_vol = sum(b[0] * b[1] for b in top_bids)
L0089:             top_ask_vol = sum(a[0] * a[1] for a in top_asks)
L0090:             bid_ask_ratio    = total_bids / total_asks
L0091:             bid_concentration = top_bid_vol / (total_bids + 1e-10)
L0092:             ask_concentration = top_ask_vol / (total_asks + 1e-10)
L0093:             bid_wall = max(top_bids, key=lambda x: x[0] * x[1])
L0094:             ask_wall = max(top_asks, key=lambda x: x[0] * x[1])
L0095:             fake_detected, fake_side, fake_conf, wall_vanished, wall_ratio =                 self._detect_fake_wall(market, bids, asks)
L0096:             if fake_detected and fake_conf >= 0.6:
L0097:                 signal     = "FAKE_WALL"
L0098:                 confidence = fake_conf
L0099:                 reason     = (
L0100:                     f"페이크월 탐지 ({fake_side.upper()}) "
L0101:                     f"신뢰도={fake_conf:.0%} 크기={wall_ratio:.1f}배"
L0102:                 )
L0103:             else:
L0104:                 signal, confidence, reason = self._classify(
L0105:                     bid_ask_ratio, spread, bid_concentration, ask_concentration
L0106:                 )
L0107:             result = OrderbookSignal(
L0108:                 market=market,
L0109:                 bid_ask_ratio=round(bid_ask_ratio, 3),
L0110:                 spread_pct=round(spread, 4),
L0111:                 bid_wall_price=bid_wall[0],
L0112:                 ask_wall_price=ask_wall[0],
L0113:                 bid_concentration=round(bid_concentration, 3),
L0114:                 ask_concentration=round(ask_concentration, 3),
L0115:                 signal=signal,
L0116:                 confidence=confidence,
L0117:                 reason=reason,
L0118:                 fake_wall_detected=fake_detected,
L0119:                 fake_wall_side=fake_side,
L0120:                 fake_wall_confidence=fake_conf,
L0121:                 wall_vanished=wall_vanished,
L0122:                 wall_size_ratio=wall_ratio,
L0123:             )
L0124:             self._update_history(market, bids, asks)
L0125:             if fake_detected:
L0126:                 logger.info(
L0127:                     f"🚨 페이크월 탐지 | {market} | {fake_side.upper()} | "
L0128:                     f"신뢰도={fake_conf:.0%} | 크기={wall_ratio:.1f}배 | "
L0129:                     f"소멸감지={wall_vanished}"
L0130:                 )
L0131:             else:
L0132:                 logger.debug(
L0133:                     f"📊 호가창 신호 | {market} | {signal} | "
L0134:                     f"bid/ask={bid_ask_ratio:.2f} | spread={spread:.3f}%"
L0135:                 )
L0136:             return result
L0137:         except Exception as e:
L0138:             logger.error(f"호가창 분석 오류 ({market}): {e}")
L0139:             return None
L0140:     def _detect_fake_wall(
L0141:         self, market: str,
L0142:         bids: List[Tuple], asks: List[Tuple]
L0143:     ) -> Tuple[bool, str, float, bool, float]:
L0144:         """
L0145:         Returns: (detected, side, confidence, vanished, size_ratio)
L0146:         """
L0147:         fake_detected = False
L0148:         fake_side     = ""
L0149:         fake_conf     = 0.0
L0150:         wall_vanished = False
L0151:         wall_ratio    = 0.0
L0152:         for side, levels in [("bid", bids), ("ask", asks)]:
L0153:             if len(levels) < 3:
L0154:                 continue
L0155:             sizes = [s for _, s in levels]
L0156:             avg_size = sum(sizes) / len(sizes) if sizes else 1e-9
L0157:             wall_candidates = [
L0158:                 (idx, price, size)
L0159:                 for idx, (price, size) in enumerate(levels)
L0160:                 if size >= avg_size * self.WALL_THR and idx < 5
L0161:             ]
L0162:             if not wall_candidates:
L0163:                 continue
L0164:             best = max(wall_candidates, key=lambda x: x[2])
L0165:             idx, price, size = best
L0166:             ratio = size / (avg_size + 1e-9)
L0167:             conf = 0.0
L0168:             history = self._wall_history.get(market, deque())
L0169:             same_side_history = [
L0170:                 e for e in history
L0171:                 if e[0] == side and abs(e[1] - price) / (price + 1e-9) < 0.005
L0172:             ]
L0173:             if len(same_side_history) <= 1:
L0174:                 conf += 0.40
L0175:             if idx <= 1:
L0176:                 conf += 0.25
L0177:             snap = self._last_snapshot.get(market)
L0178:             if snap:
L0179:                 prev_levels = snap["bids"] if side == "bid" else snap["asks"]
L0180:                 prev_same = [s for p, s in prev_levels if abs(p - price) / (price + 1e-9) < 0.002]
L0181:                 if prev_same and size / (prev_same[0] + 1e-9) >= 3.0:
L0182:                     conf += 0.20
L0183:             if history:
L0184:                 last = list(history)[-1]
L0185:                 last_side, last_price, last_size, last_ts = last
L0186:                 elapsed = time.time() - last_ts
L0187:                 if (last_side == side and
L0188:                         abs(last_price - price) / (price + 1e-9) > 0.005 and
L0189:                         elapsed < self.FAKE_WALL_VANISH_SEC):
L0190:                     wall_vanished = True
L0191:                     conf += 0.15
L0192:             conf = min(conf, 1.0)
L0193:             if conf > fake_conf:
L0194:                 fake_conf     = conf
L0195:                 fake_side     = side
L0196:                 wall_ratio    = ratio
L0197:                 fake_detected = conf >= 0.5
L0198:         return fake_detected, fake_side, fake_conf, wall_vanished, wall_ratio
L0199:     def _update_history(self, market: str, bids: List, asks: List):
L0200:         """벽 히스토리 업데이트"""
L0201:         if market not in self._wall_history:
L0202:             self._wall_history[market] = deque(maxlen=self.HISTORY_MAXLEN)
L0203:         now = time.time()
L0204:         for side, levels in [("bid", bids), ("ask", asks)]:
L0205:             if not levels:
L0206:                 continue
L0207:             sizes = [s for _, s in levels]
L0208:             avg_size = sum(sizes) / len(sizes) if sizes else 1e-9
L0209:             walls = [
L0210:                 (idx, p, s) for idx, (p, s) in enumerate(levels)
L0211:                 if s >= avg_size * self.WALL_THR and idx < 5
L0212:             ]
L0213:             if walls:
L0214:                 best = max(walls, key=lambda x: x[2])
L0215:                 self._wall_history[market].append(
L0216:                     (side, best[1], best[2], now)
L0217:                 )
L0218:         self._last_snapshot[market] = {
L0219:             "bids": bids, "asks": asks, "ts": now
L0220:         }
L0221:     def _classify(
L0222:         self,
L0223:         bid_ask_ratio: float,
L0224:         spread_pct: float,
L0225:         bid_conc: float,
L0226:         ask_conc: float,
L0227:     ) -> Tuple[str, float, str]:
L0228:         reasons = []
L0229:         if spread_pct > self.SPREAD_WIDE_PCT:
L0230:             return "NEUTRAL", 0.3, f"스프레드 과다 {spread_pct:.3f}%"
L0231:         confidence = 0.5
L0232:         if bid_ask_ratio >= self.BUY_PRESSURE_RATIO:
L0233:             boost = min((bid_ask_ratio - self.BUY_PRESSURE_RATIO) * 0.2, 0.3)
L0234:             confidence = min(0.5 + boost + bid_conc * 0.2, 0.90)
L0235:             reasons.append(f"매수벽 {bid_ask_ratio:.1f}배 우세")
L0236:             if bid_conc > 0.6:
L0237:                 reasons.append(f"상위5단계 집중 {bid_conc:.0%}")
L0238:             return "BUY_PRESSURE", confidence, " | ".join(reasons)
L0239:         elif 1 / bid_ask_ratio >= self.SELL_PRESSURE_RATIO:
L0240:             inv_ratio = 1 / bid_ask_ratio
L0241:             boost = min((inv_ratio - self.SELL_PRESSURE_RATIO) * 0.2, 0.3)
L0242:             confidence = min(0.5 + boost + ask_conc * 0.2, 0.90)
L0243:             reasons.append(f"매도벽 {inv_ratio:.1f}배 우세")
L0244:             if ask_conc > 0.6:
L0245:                 reasons.append(f"상위5단계 집중 {ask_conc:.0%}")
L0246:             return "SELL_PRESSURE", confidence, " | ".join(reasons)
L0247:         return "NEUTRAL", 0.5, f"bid/ask={bid_ask_ratio:.2f} (중립)"
L0248:     def get_confidence_adjustment(
L0249:         self, signal: Optional[OrderbookSignal], trade_side: str = "BUY"
L0250:     ) -> float:
L0251:         if signal is None:
L0252:             return 0.0
L0253:         if signal.fake_wall_detected and trade_side == "BUY":
L0254:             return -0.20
L0255:         if trade_side == "BUY":
L0256:             if signal.signal == "BUY_PRESSURE":
L0257:                 return min((signal.confidence - 0.5) * 0.3, 0.15)
L0258:             elif signal.signal == "SELL_PRESSURE":
L0259:                 return max(-(signal.confidence - 0.5) * 0.3, -0.15)
L0260:         elif trade_side == "SELL":
L0261:             if signal.signal == "SELL_PRESSURE":
L0262:                 return min((signal.confidence - 0.5) * 0.3, 0.15)
L0263:             elif signal.signal == "BUY_PRESSURE":
L0264:                 return max(-(signal.confidence - 0.5) * 0.3, -0.15)
L0265:         return 0.0
L0266:     def can_buy(
L0267:         self, signal: Optional[OrderbookSignal]
L0268:     ) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
L0269:         if signal is None:
L0270:             return True, "호가창 데이터 없음 (통과)"
L0271:         if signal.fake_wall_detected and signal.fake_wall_confidence >= 0.6:
L0272:             return False, (
L0273:                 f"페이크월 차단 ({signal.fake_wall_side.upper()}) "
L0274:                 f"신뢰도={signal.fake_wall_confidence:.0%}"
L0275:             )
L0276:         if signal.wall_vanished:
L0277:             return False, "벽 소멸 감지 → 스마트머니 이탈 가능"
L0278:         if signal.spread_pct > self.SPREAD_WIDE_PCT:
L0279:             return False, f"스프레드 과다 {signal.spread_pct:.3f}%"
L0280:         if signal.signal == "SELL_PRESSURE" and signal.confidence >= 0.75:
L0281:             return False, f"강한 매도 압력 (신뢰도={signal.confidence:.2f})"
L0282:         return True, "OK"

FILE: signals/mtf_signal_merger.py  (5.1KB → 4.9KB)

L0001: """
L0002: Apex Bot - 멀티 타임프레임 신호 합산기 (M3)
L0003: 6개 TF 신호를 가중 합산하여 최종 방향 결정
L0004: """
L0005: import pandas as pd
L0006: import numpy as np
L0007: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
L0008: from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
L0009: from enum import Enum
L0010: from loguru import logger
L0011: class TFDirection(Enum):
L0012:     STRONG_UP   =  2
L0013:     UP          =  1
L0014:     NEUTRAL     =  0
L0015:     DOWN        = -1
L0016:     STRONG_DOWN = -2
L0017: @dataclass
L0018: class TFSignal:
L0019:     timeframe:  str
L0020:     direction:  TFDirection
L0021:     strength:   float
L0022:     ema_trend:  str
L0023:     rsi:        float
L0024:     weight:     float
L0025: @dataclass
L0026: class MTFResult:
L0027:     combined_score:  float
L0028:     final_direction: TFDirection
L0029:     allow_buy:       bool
L0030:     allow_sell:      bool
L0031:     tf_signals:      List[TFSignal] = field(default_factory=list)
L0032:     dominant_tf:     str = ""
L0033:     reason:          str = ""
L0034: TF_WEIGHTS: Dict[str, float] = {
L0035:     "1d":  0.35,
L0036:     "4h":  0.25,
L0037:     "1h":  0.20,
L0038:     "15m": 0.12,
L0039:     "5m":  0.05,
L0040:     "1m":  0.03,
L0041: }
L0042: class MTFSignalMerger:
L0043:     """멀티 타임프레임 신호 합산기"""
L0044:     def __init__(self, weights: Dict[str, float] = None):
L0045:         self.weights = weights or TF_WEIGHTS
L0046:         logger.info(f"✅ MTFSignalMerger 초기화 | TF: {list(self.weights.keys())}")
L0047:     def analyze(self, tf_dataframes: Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]) -> MTFResult:
L0048:         """
L0049:         tf_dataframes: {"1d": df_daily, "4h": df_4h, ...}
L0050:         각 df는 최소 close, ema_20, ema_50, ema_200, rsi 컬럼 필요
L0051:         """
L0052:         tf_signals = []
L0053:         for tf, df in tf_dataframes.items():
L0054:             if df is None or len(df) < 5:
L0055:                 continue
L0056:             sig = self._analyze_single_tf(tf, df)
L0057:             tf_signals.append(sig)
L0058:         if not tf_signals:
L0059:             return MTFResult(
L0060:                 combined_score  = 0.0,
L0061:                 final_direction = TFDirection.NEUTRAL,
L0062:                 allow_buy       = False,
L0063:                 allow_sell      = False,
L0064:                 reason          = "데이터 없음",
L0065:             )
L0066:         return self._merge(tf_signals)
L0067:     def _analyze_single_tf(self, tf: str, df: pd.DataFrame) -> TFSignal:
L0068:         last    = df.iloc[-1]
L0069:         close   = float(last.get("close", 0))
L0070:         ema20   = float(last.get("ema_20",  close))
L0071:         ema50   = float(last.get("ema_50",  close))
L0072:         ema200  = float(last.get("ema_200", close))
L0073:         rsi     = float(last.get("rsi",     50))
L0074:         weight  = self.weights.get(tf, 0.1)
L0075:         if close > ema20 > ema50 > ema200:
L0076:             direction  = TFDirection.STRONG_UP
L0077:             ema_trend  = "UP"
L0078:             strength   = min(1.0, (close - ema200) / ema200 * 10)
L0079:         elif close > ema50:
L0080:             direction  = TFDirection.UP
L0081:             ema_trend  = "UP"
L0082:             strength   = 0.6
L0083:         elif close < ema20 < ema50 < ema200:
L0084:             direction  = TFDirection.STRONG_DOWN
L0085:             ema_trend  = "DOWN"
L0086:             strength   = min(1.0, (ema200 - close) / ema200 * 10)
L0087:         elif close < ema50:
L0088:             direction  = TFDirection.DOWN
L0089:             ema_trend  = "DOWN"
L0090:             strength   = 0.6
L0091:         else:
L0092:             direction  = TFDirection.NEUTRAL
L0093:             ema_trend  = "FLAT"
L0094:             strength   = 0.3
L0095:         return TFSignal(
L0096:             timeframe  = tf,
L0097:             direction  = direction,
L0098:             strength   = strength,
L0099:             ema_trend  = ema_trend,
L0100:             rsi        = rsi,
L0101:             weight     = weight,
L0102:         )
L0103:     def _merge(self, signals: List[TFSignal]) -> MTFResult:
L0104:         total_weight = sum(s.weight for s in signals)
L0105:         score        = sum(
L0106:             s.direction.value * s.strength * s.weight
L0107:             for s in signals
L0108:         ) / (total_weight or 1)
L0109:         higher_tfs   = [s for s in signals if s.timeframe in ("1d", "4h")]
L0110:         higher_down  = any(s.direction in (TFDirection.DOWN, TFDirection.STRONG_DOWN)
L0111:                            for s in higher_tfs)
L0112:         higher_up    = any(s.direction in (TFDirection.UP, TFDirection.STRONG_UP)
L0113:                            for s in higher_tfs)
L0114:         allow_buy  = score > 0.3 and not higher_down
L0115:         allow_sell = score < -0.3 and not higher_up
L0116:         if score > 1.0:
L0117:             final = TFDirection.STRONG_UP
L0118:         elif score > 0.3:
L0119:             final = TFDirection.UP
L0120:         elif score < -1.0:
L0121:             final = TFDirection.STRONG_DOWN
L0122:         elif score < -0.3:
L0123:             final = TFDirection.DOWN
L0124:         else:
L0125:             final = TFDirection.NEUTRAL
L0126:         dominant = max(signals, key=lambda s: s.weight * abs(s.direction.value))
L0127:         return MTFResult(
L0128:             combined_score  = score,
L0129:             final_direction = final,
L0130:             allow_buy       = allow_buy,
L0131:             allow_sell      = allow_sell,
L0132:             tf_signals      = signals,
L0133:             dominant_tf     = dominant.timeframe,
L0134:             reason          = (
L0135:                 f"MTF합산={score:.2f} | 지배TF={dominant.timeframe} | "
L0136:                 f"BUY={'✅' if allow_buy else '❌'} SELL={'✅' if allow_sell else '❌'}"
L0137:             ),
L0138:         )

L0019: class RestCollector:
L0020:     """
L0021:     업비트 REST API 데이터 수집기
L0022:     - OHLCV (분봉/일봉/주봉)
L0023:     - 현재가 / 호가 / 체결내역
L0024:     - 자동 레이트 리밋 (초당 10회)
L0025:     - pyupbit fallback → aiohttp 직접 호출
L0026:     """
L0027:     BASE_URL = "https://api.upbit.com/v1"
L0028:     def __init__(self):
L0029:         self.settings = get_settings()
L0030:         self._limiter = RateLimiter(calls_per_second=5)
L0031:         self._session = None
L0032:         self._cache: Dict[str, Dict] = {}
L0033:     async def get_ohlcv(
L0034:         self, market: str, interval: str = "minute60",
L0035:         count: int = 200
L0036:     ) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:
L0037:         """
L0038:         OHLCV 캔들 데이터 조회
L0039:         Args:
L0040:             market: 'KRW-BTC'
L0041:             interval: 'minute1'|'minute5'|'minute15'|'minute60'|'minute240'|'day'|'week'
L0042:             count: 최대 200개 (업비트 제한)
L0043:         """
L0044:         await self._limiter.acquire()
L0045:         cache_key = f"{market}_{interval}_{count}"
L0046:         if cache_key in self._cache:
L0047:             cached = self._cache[cache_key]
L0048:             if time.time() - cached["ts"] < 60:
L0049:                 return cached["data"]
L0050:         if PYUPBIT_OK:
L0051:             try:
L0052:                 df = await asyncio.get_event_loop().run_in_executor(
L0053:                     None, pyupbit.get_ohlcv, market, interval, count
L0054:                 )
L0055:                 if df is not None and not df.empty:
L0056:                     df = self._normalize_df(df)
L0057:                     self._cache[cache_key] = {"ts": time.time(), "data": df}
L0058:                     return df
L0059:             except Exception as e:
L0060:                 logger.warning(f"pyupbit OHLCV 오류 ({market}): {e}")
L0061:         return await self._fetch_ohlcv_api(market, interval, count)
L0062:     @async_retry(max_attempts=3, delay=1.0)
L0063:     async def _fetch_ohlcv_api(self, market: str, interval: str, count: int) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:
L0064:         """aiohttp 직접 OHLCV 조회"""
L0065:         try:
L0066:             import aiohttp
L0067:             endpoint, params = self._build_candle_request(market, interval, count)
L0068:             async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
L0069:                 async with session.get(endpoint, params=params) as resp:
L0070:                     if resp.status == 429:
L0071:                         logger.warning(f"API 429 Rate Limit ({market}) → 1초 대기")
L0072:                         await asyncio.sleep(1.0)
L0073:                         return None
L0074:                     if resp.status != 200:
L0075:                         logger.error(f"API 오류 ({resp.status}): {market}")
L0076:                         return None
L0077:                     data = await resp.json()
L0078:             if not data:
L0079:                 return None
L0080:             df = pd.DataFrame(data)
L0081:             df = df.rename(columns={
L0082:                 "candle_date_time_kst": "datetime",
L0083:                 "opening_price": "open",
L0084:                 "high_price": "high",
L0085:                 "low_price": "low",
L0086:                 "trade_price": "close",
L0087:                 "candle_acc_trade_volume": "volume",
L0088:             })
L0089:             df["datetime"] = pd.to_datetime(df["datetime"])
L0090:             df = df.set_index("datetime").sort_index()
L0091:             df = df[["open", "high", "low", "close", "volume"]].astype(float)
L0092:             return df
L0093:         except Exception as e:
L0094:             logger.error(f"OHLCV API 직접 호출 실패 ({market}): {e}")
L0095:             return None
L0096:     def _build_candle_request(self, market: str, interval: str, count: int):
L0097:         """업비트 API 엔드포인트 빌드"""
L0098:         params = {"market": market, "count": min(count, 200)}
L0099:         if interval.startswith("minute"):
L0100:             unit = interval.replace("minute", "")
L0101:             endpoint = f"{self.BASE_URL}/candles/minutes/{unit}"
L0102:         elif interval == "day":
L0103:             endpoint = f"{self.BASE_URL}/candles/days"
L0104:         elif interval == "week":
L0105:             endpoint = f"{self.BASE_URL}/candles/weeks"
L0106:         else:
L0107:             endpoint = f"{self.BASE_URL}/candles/minutes/60"
L0108:         return endpoint, params
L0109:     async def get_ticker(self, markets: List[str]) -> Optional[List[Dict]]:
L0110:         """현재가 (다중 코인)"""
L0111:         await self._limiter.acquire()
L0112:         if PYUPBIT_OK:
L0113:             try:
L0114:                 market_str = ",".join(markets)
L0115:                 result = await asyncio.get_event_loop().run_in_executor(
L0116:                     None, pyupbit.get_tickers_krw_ticker, market_str
L0117:                 )
L0118:                 return result
L0119:             except Exception:
L0120:                 pass
L0121:         return await self._fetch_ticker_api(markets)
L0122:     async def _fetch_ticker_api(self, markets: List[str]) -> Optional[List[Dict]]:
L0123:         try:
L0124:             import aiohttp
L0125:             market_str = ",".join(markets)
L0126:             url = f"{self.BASE_URL}/ticker"
L0127:             async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
L0128:                 async with session.get(url, params={"markets": market_str}) as resp:
L0129:                     if resp.status == 200:
L0130:                         return await resp.json()
L0131:         except Exception as e:
L0132:             logger.error(f"티커 조회 실패: {e}")
L0133:         return None
L0134:     async def get_orderbook(self, market: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
L0135:         """호가창 조회"""
L0136:         await self._limiter.acquire()
L0137:         try:
L0138:             import aiohttp
L0139:             url = f"{self.BASE_URL}/orderbook"
L0140:             async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
L0141:                 async with session.get(url, params={"markets": market}) as resp:
L0142:                     if resp.status == 200:
L0143:                         data = await resp.json()
L0144:                         return data[0] if data else None
L0145:         except Exception as e:
L0146:             logger.error(f"호가 조회 실패 ({market}): {e}")
L0147:         return None
L0148:     async def get_multiple_ohlcv(
L0149:         self, markets: List[str], interval: str = "minute60", count: int = 200
L0150:     ) -> Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]:
L0151:         """다중 코인 OHLCV 병렬 수집"""
L0152:         tasks = [self.get_ohlcv(m, interval, count) for m in markets]
L0153:         results = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
L0154:         return {
L0155:             market: df
L0156:             for market, df in zip(markets, results)
L0157:             if df is not None and not isinstance(df, Exception)
L0158:         }
L0159:     @staticmethod
L0160:     def _normalize_df(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
L0161:         """pyupbit DataFrame 정규화"""
L0162:         df.index = pd.to_datetime(df.index)
L0163:         df.index.name = "datetime"
L0164:         for col in ["open", "high", "low", "close", "volume"]:
L0165:             if col in df.columns:
L0166:                 df[col] = df[col].astype(float)
L0167:         return df.sort_index()

L0001: """
L0002: APEX BOT - 업비트 WebSocket 실시간 데이터 수집기

L0006: - Rate Limit 준수 (초당 5회 연결, 최대 5개 동시)
L0007: """
L0008: import asyncio
L0009: import json
L0010: import uuid
L0011: import time
L0012: from datetime import datetime
L0013: from typing import Callable, List, Optional, Dict
L0014: import websockets
L0015: from websockets.exceptions import ConnectionClosed, WebSocketException
L0016: import logging
L0017: logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
L0018: class UpbitWebSocketCollector:
L0019:     """
L0020:     업비트 WebSocket 수집기
L0021:     wss://api.upbit.com/websocket/v1 연결
L0022:     """
L0023:     WS_URL = "wss://api.upbit.com/websocket/v1"
L0024:     PING_INTERVAL = 30
L0025:     RECONNECT_DELAY = 5
L0026:     MAX_RECONNECT_ATTEMPTS = 10
L0027:     def __init__(self, markets: List[str], on_message: Callable, on_error: Optional[Callable] = None):
L0028:         """
L0029:         Args:
L0030:             markets: 구독할 마켓 리스트 (예: ["KRW-BTC", "KRW-ETH"])
L0031:             on_message: 메시지 수신 콜백 (async)
L0032:             on_error: 에러 콜백 (async)
L0033:         """
L0034:         self.markets = markets
L0035:         self.on_message = on_message
L0036:         self.on_error = on_error
L0037:         self._ws: Optional[websockets.WebSocketClientProtocol] = None
L0038:         self._running = False
L0039:         self._reconnect_count = 0
L0040:         self._last_message_time = time.time()
L0041:         self._message_count = 0
L0042:         self._subscription_types: List[str] = []
L0043:     def subscribe_ticker(self) -> "UpbitWebSocketCollector":
L0044:         """현재가(ticker) 구독"""
L0045:         self._subscription_types.append("ticker")
L0046:         return self
L0047:     def subscribe_trade(self) -> "UpbitWebSocketCollector":
L0048:         """체결(trade) 구독"""
L0049:         self._subscription_types.append("trade")
L0050:         return self
L0051:     def subscribe_orderbook(self) -> "UpbitWebSocketCollector":
L0052:         """호가(orderbook) 구독"""
L0053:         self._subscription_types.append("orderbook")
L0054:         return self
L0055:     def _build_subscribe_message(self) -> str:
L0056:         """업비트 WebSocket 구독 메시지 생성"""
L0057:         ticket = str(uuid.uuid4())
L0058:         message = [{"ticket": ticket}]
L0059:         for sub_type in self._subscription_types:
L0060:             entry = {"type": sub_type, "codes": self.markets}
L0061:             if sub_type == "trade":
L0062:                 entry["isOnlyRealtime"] = True
L0063:             message.append(entry)
L0064:         message.append({"format": "SIMPLE"})
L0065:         return json.dumps(message)
L0066:     async def connect(self):
L0067:         """WebSocket 연결 및 구독"""
L0068:         subscribe_msg = self._build_subscribe_message()
L0069:         async with websockets.connect(
L0070:             self.WS_URL,
L0071:             ping_interval=self.PING_INTERVAL,
L0072:             ping_timeout=10,
L0073:             close_timeout=10,
L0074:             max_size=2**20,
L0075:             extra_headers={"User-Agent": "ApexBot/1.0"}
L0076:         ) as ws:
L0077:             self._ws = ws
L0078:             self._reconnect_count = 0
L0079:             logger.info(f"✅ WebSocket 연결 성공 | 마켓: {len(self.markets)}개")
L0080:             await ws.send(subscribe_msg)
L0081:             logger.info(f"📡 구독 시작: {self._subscription_types}")
L0082:             async for raw_message in ws:
L0083:                 if not self._running:
L0084:                     break
L0085:                 try:
L0086:                     self._last_message_time = time.time()
L0087:                     self._message_count += 1
L0088:                     if isinstance(raw_message, bytes):
L0089:                         data = json.loads(raw_message.decode("utf-8"))
L0090:                     else:
L0091:                         data = json.loads(raw_message)
L0092:                     await self.on_message(data)
L0093:                 except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
L0094:                     logger.warning(f"⚠️ JSON 파싱 오류: {e}")
L0095:                 except Exception as e:
L0096:                     logger.error(f"❌ 메시지 처리 오류: {e}")
L0097:                     if self.on_error:
L0098:                         await self.on_error(e)
L0099:     async def run(self):
L0100:         """자동 재연결을 포함한 실행 루프"""
L0101:         self._running = True
L0102:         logger.info("🚀 WebSocket 수집기 시작")
L0103:         while self._running:
L0104:             try:
L0105:                 await self.connect()
L0106:             except ConnectionClosed as e:
L0107:                 if not self._running:
L0108:                     break
L0109:                 logger.warning(f"⚠️ WebSocket 연결 끊김: {e} | 재연결 중...")
L0110:             except WebSocketException as e:
L0111:                 logger.error(f"❌ WebSocket 오류: {e}")
L0112:             except Exception as e:
L0113:                 logger.error(f"❌ 예상치 못한 오류: {e}")
L0114:             if not self._running:
L0115:                 break
L0116:             self._reconnect_count += 1
L0117:             if self._reconnect_count > self.MAX_RECONNECT_ATTEMPTS:
L0118:                 logger.critical("🚨 최대 재연결 시도 초과!")
L0119:                 if self.on_error:
L0120:                     await self.on_error(Exception("Max reconnect attempts exceeded"))
L0121:                 break
L0122:             delay = min(self.RECONNECT_DELAY * (2 ** min(self._reconnect_count - 1, 5)), 60)
L0123:             logger.info(f"🔄 {delay}초 후 재연결 시도 ({self._reconnect_count}/{self.MAX_RECONNECT_ATTEMPTS})")
L0124:             await asyncio.sleep(delay)
L0125:     async def stop(self):
L0126:         """수집기 중지"""
L0127:         self._running = False
L0128:         if self._ws:
L0129:             await self._ws.close()
L0130:         logger.info(f"🛑 WebSocket 수집기 중지 (수신 메시지: {self._message_count}개)")
L0131:     @property
L0132:     def is_healthy(self) -> bool:
L0133:         """연결 상태 확인 (60초 내 메시지 수신 여부)"""
L0134:         return (time.time() - self._last_message_time) < 60
L0135:     @property
L0136:     def stats(self) -> dict:
L0137:         return {
L0138:             "running": self._running,
L0139:             "message_count": self._message_count,
L0140:             "reconnect_count": self._reconnect_count,
L0141:             "last_message_seconds_ago": round(time.time() - self._last_message_time, 1),
L0142:             "is_healthy": self.is_healthy,
L0143:             "markets": len(self.markets),
L0144:         }
L0145: class MultiStreamCollector:
L0146:     """
L0147:     다중 스트림 수집기
L0148:     업비트 제한(최대 5개 동시 연결)을 준수하며
L0149:     많은 코인을 여러 WebSocket으로 분산 처리
L0150:     """
L0151:     MAX_MARKETS_PER_STREAM = 20
L0152:     def __init__(self, all_markets: List[str], on_candle: Callable,
L0153:                  on_trade: Callable, on_orderbook: Callable):
L0154:         self.all_markets = all_markets
L0155:         self.on_candle = on_candle
L0156:         self.on_trade = on_trade
L0157:         self.on_orderbook = on_orderbook
L0158:         self._collectors: List[UpbitWebSocketCollector] = []
L0159:         self._tasks: List[asyncio.Task] = []
L0160:     def _chunk_markets(self) -> List[List[str]]:
L0161:         """마켓 리스트를 청크로 분할"""
L0162:         chunks = []
L0163:         for i in range(0, len(self.all_markets), self.MAX_MARKETS_PER_STREAM):
L0164:             chunks.append(self.all_markets[i:i + self.MAX_MARKETS_PER_STREAM])
L0165:         return chunks
L0166:     async def _message_router(self, data: dict):
L0167:         """수신 메시지를 타입에 따라 라우팅"""
L0168:         msg_type = data.get("ty", data.get("type", ""))
L0169:         if msg_type == "ticker":
L0170:             await self.on_candle(data)
L0171:         elif msg_type == "trade":
L0172:             await self.on_trade(data)
L0173:         elif msg_type == "orderbook":
L0174:             await self.on_orderbook(data)
L0175:     async def start(self):
L0176:         """모든 스트림 시작"""
L0177:         chunks = self._chunk_markets()
L0178:         logger.info(f"📡 {len(chunks)}개 스트림으로 {len(self.all_markets)}개 마켓 수집 시작")
L0179:         for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks):
L0180:             collector = (
L0181:                 UpbitWebSocketCollector(chunk, self._message_router)
L0182:                 .subscribe_ticker()
L0183:                 .subscribe_trade()
L0184:                 .subscribe_orderbook()
L0185:             )
L0186:             self._collectors.append(collector)
L0187:             task = asyncio.create_task(collector.run(), name=f"stream_{i}")
L0188:             self._tasks.append(task)
L0189:             await asyncio.sleep(0.3)
L0190:     async def stop(self):
L0191:         """모든 스트림 중지"""
L0192:         for collector in self._collectors:
L0193:             await collector.stop()
L0194:         for task in self._tasks:
L0195:             task.cancel()
L0196:     def get_health_status(self) -> List[dict]:
L0197:         return [c.stats for c in self._collectors]

L0001: """

L0006:          .iloc[i] = 직접 할당 → 명시적 .copy() + .at[] 방식으로 변경
L0007:        - 기타 iloc 할당 방어 처리
L0008: """
L0009: import asyncio
L0010: from typing import Dict, Optional, List
L0011: import pandas as pd
L0012: import numpy as np
L0013: from loguru import logger
L0014: from config.settings import get_settings
L0015: class CandleProcessor:
L0016:     """
L0017:     멀티 타임프레임 캔들 데이터 전처리기
L0018:     - 업비트 OHLCV 데이터 정규화
L0019:     - 기술지표 일괄 계산
L0020:     - 타임프레임 동기화
L0021:     """
L0022:     TIMEFRAME_MAP = {
L0023:         "1": "minute1", "5": "minute5", "15": "minute15",
L0024:         "60": "minute60", "240": "minute240", "1440": "day",
L0025:     }
L0026:     def __init__(self):
L0027:         self.settings = get_settings()
L0028:         self._candle_cache: Dict[str, Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]] = {}
L0029:         self._lock = asyncio.Lock()
L0030:         try:
L0031:             import pandas_ta as ta
L0032:             self._ta = ta
L0033:             logger.info("✅ pandas_ta 로드 성공")
L0034:         except ImportError:
L0035:             self._ta = None
L0036:             logger.warning("⚠️ pandas_ta 미설치 - 기본 지표만 사용")
L0037:     async def process(
L0038:         self, market: str, raw_df: pd.DataFrame, timeframe: str = "60"
L0039:     ) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:
L0040:         """원시 캔들 → 지표 포함 DataFrame 반환"""
L0041:         if raw_df is None or raw_df.empty:
L0042:             return None
L0043:         try:
L0044:             df = self._normalize(raw_df.copy())
L0045:             df = self._add_indicators(df)
L0046:             df = self._add_volume_analysis(df)
L0047:             df = self._add_candle_patterns(df)
L0048:             df = df.dropna(subset=["ema20", "rsi"])
L0049:             async with self._lock:
L0050:                 if market not in self._candle_cache:
L0051:                     self._candle_cache[market] = {}
L0052:                 max_c = self.settings.database.cache_max_candles
L0053:                 self._candle_cache[market][timeframe] = df.tail(max_c)
L0054:             return df
L0055:         except Exception as e:
L0056:             logger.error(f"캔들 처리 실패 ({market}/{timeframe}): {e}")
L0057:             return None
L0058:     def get_cached(
L0059:         self, market: str, timeframe: str = "60"
L0060:     ) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:
L0061:         return self._candle_cache.get(market, {}).get(timeframe)
L0062:     def _normalize(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
L0063:         for col in ["open", "high", "low", "close", "volume"]:
L0064:             if col not in df.columns:
L0065:                 raise ValueError(f"필수 컬럼 누락: {col}")
L0066:         df = df.sort_index()
L0067:         df = df.astype({
L0068:             "open": float, "high": float, "low": float,
L0069:             "close": float, "volume": float,
L0070:         })
L0071:         return df
L0072:     def _add_indicators(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
L0073:         c, h, l, v = df["close"], df["high"], df["low"], df["volume"]
L0074:         for p in [5, 10, 20, 50, 100, 200]:
L0075:             df[f"ema{p}"] = c.ewm(span=p, adjust=False).mean()
L0076:             df[f"sma{p}"] = c.rolling(p).mean()
L0077:         e12 = c.ewm(span=12, adjust=False).mean()
L0078:         e26 = c.ewm(span=26, adjust=False).mean()
L0079:         df["macd"]        = e12 - e26
L0080:         df["macd_signal"] = df["macd"].ewm(span=9, adjust=False).mean()
L0081:         df["macd_hist"]   = df["macd"] - df["macd_signal"]
L0082:         delta = c.diff()
L0083:         gain  = delta.clip(lower=0).rolling(14).mean()
L0084:         loss  = (-delta.clip(upper=0)).rolling(14).mean()
L0085:         rs    = gain / loss.replace(0, np.nan)
L0086:         df["rsi"]      = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))
L0087:         df["rsi_fast"] = self._calc_rsi(c, 7)
L0088:         df["rsi_slow"] = self._calc_rsi(c, 21)
L0089:         bb_mid = c.rolling(20).mean()
L0090:         bb_std = c.rolling(20).std()
L0091:         df["bb_upper"] = bb_mid + 2 * bb_std
L0092:         df["bb_mid"]   = bb_mid
L0093:         df["bb_lower"] = bb_mid - 2 * bb_std
L0094:         df["bb_width"] = (df["bb_upper"] - df["bb_lower"]) / (bb_mid + 1e-10)
L0095:         df["bb_pct"]   = (c - df["bb_lower"]) / (
L0096:             df["bb_upper"] - df["bb_lower"] + 1e-10
L0097:         )
L0098:         tr = pd.concat([
L0099:             h - l,
L0100:             (h - c.shift()).abs(),
L0101:             (l - c.shift()).abs(),
L0102:         ], axis=1).max(axis=1)
L0103:         df["atr"]     = tr.ewm(span=14, adjust=False).mean()
L0104:         df["atr_pct"] = df["atr"] / (c + 1e-10) * 100
L0105:         low14  = l.rolling(14).min()
L0106:         high14 = h.rolling(14).max()
L0107:         df["stoch_k"] = 100 * (c - low14) / (high14 - low14 + 1e-10)
L0108:         df["stoch_d"] = df["stoch_k"].rolling(3).mean()
L0109:         tp        = (h + l + c) / 3
L0110:         df["vwap"] = (tp * v).cumsum() / v.cumsum()
L0111:         df["supertrend"], df["supertrend_dir"] = self._calc_supertrend(df)
L0112:         df["obv"]     = (np.sign(c.diff()) * v).fillna(0).cumsum()
L0113:         df["obv_ema"] = df["obv"].ewm(span=20, adjust=False).mean()
L0114:         df["adx"], df["di_plus"], df["di_minus"] = self._calc_adx(df)
L0115:         tp2       = (h + l + c) / 3
L0116:         df["cci"] = (tp2 - tp2.rolling(20).mean()) / (
L0117:             0.015 * tp2.rolling(20).std() + 1e-10
L0118:         )
L0119:         df["willr"] = -100 * (h.rolling(14).max() - c) / (
L0120:             h.rolling(14).max() - l.rolling(14).min() + 1e-10
L0121:         )
L0122:         df["ich_tenkan"]   = (h.rolling(9).max()  + l.rolling(9).min())  / 2
L0123:         df["ich_kijun"]    = (h.rolling(26).max() + l.rolling(26).min()) / 2
L0124:         df["ich_senkou_a"] = ((df["ich_tenkan"] + df["ich_kijun"]) / 2).shift(26)
L0125:         df["ich_senkou_b"] = (
L0126:             (h.rolling(52).max() + l.rolling(52).min()) / 2
L0127:         ).shift(26)
L0128:         df["ich_chikou"]   = c.shift(-26)
L0129:         return df
L0130:     def _add_volume_analysis(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
L0131:         v = df["volume"]
L0132:         df["vol_sma20"] = v.rolling(20).mean()
L0133:         df["vol_ratio"] = v / (df["vol_sma20"].replace(0, np.nan))
L0134:         df["vol_spike"] = df["vol_ratio"] > 2.0
L0135:         df["vol_trend"] = v.rolling(5).mean() > v.rolling(20).mean()
L0136:         tp     = (df["high"] + df["low"] + df["close"]) / 3
L0137:         mf     = tp * v
L0138:         pos_mf = mf.where(tp > tp.shift(), 0).rolling(14).sum()
L0139:         neg_mf = mf.where(tp < tp.shift(), 0).rolling(14).sum()
L0140:         df["mfi"] = 100 - (100 / (1 + pos_mf / (neg_mf.replace(0, np.nan))))
L0141:         return df
L0142:     def _add_candle_patterns(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
L0143:         o, h, l, c = df["open"], df["high"], df["low"], df["close"]
L0144:         body        = abs(c - o)
L0145:         upper_wick  = h - c.where(c > o, o)
L0146:         lower_wick  = c.where(c < o, o) - l
L0147:         df["doji"]             = body < (h - l) * 0.1
L0148:         df["hammer"]           = (lower_wick > body * 2) & (upper_wick < body * 0.5)
L0149:         df["inverted_hammer"]  = (upper_wick > body * 2) & (lower_wick < body * 0.5)
L0150:         df["bullish"]          = c > o
L0151:         df["bearish"]          = c < o
L0152:         df["bull_engulf"]      = (
L0153:             df["bearish"].shift(1) & df["bullish"] &
L0154:             (o < c.shift(1)) & (c > o.shift(1))
L0155:         )
L0156:         df["squeeze"] = body < body.rolling(10).mean() * 0.5
L0157:         return df
L0158:     @staticmethod
L0159:     def _calc_rsi(series: pd.Series, period: int = 14) -> pd.Series:
L0160:         delta = series.diff()
L0161:         gain  = delta.clip(lower=0).rolling(period).mean()
L0162:         loss  = (-delta.clip(upper=0)).rolling(period).mean()
L0163:         rs    = gain / loss.replace(0, np.nan)
L0164:         return 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))
L0165:     @staticmethod
L0166:     def _calc_supertrend(
L0167:         df: pd.DataFrame, period: int = 10, multiplier: float = 3.0
L0168:     ):
L0169:         """
L0170:         ✅ FIX: pandas CoW 경고 없는 슈퍼트렌드 계산
L0171:         .iloc[i] = 직접 할당 제거 → numpy 배열 기반으로 재구현
L0172:         """
L0173:         atr = df["atr"]
L0174:         hl2 = (df["high"] + df["low"]) / 2
L0175:         upper_band = (hl2 + multiplier * atr).values
L0176:         lower_band = (hl2 - multiplier * atr).values
L0177:         close      = df["close"].values
L0178:         n          = len(close)
L0179:         supertrend = np.full(n, np.nan)
L0180:         direction  = np.ones(n)
L0181:         first_valid = atr.first_valid_index()
L0182:         start = df.index.get_loc(first_valid) if first_valid is not None else 1
L0183:         for i in range(start, n):
L0184:             prev_st  = supertrend[i - 1] if i > 0 and not np.isnan(supertrend[i - 1]) else lower_band[i]
L0185:             prev_dir = direction[i - 1] if i > 0 else 1
L0186:             if close[i] > prev_st:
L0187:                 direction[i]  = 1
L0188:                 supertrend[i] = max(lower_band[i], prev_st)
L0189:             else:
L0190:                 direction[i]  = -1
L0191:                 supertrend[i] = min(upper_band[i], prev_st)
L0192:         st_series  = pd.Series(supertrend, index=df.index)
L0193:         dir_series = pd.Series(direction,  index=df.index)
L0194:         return st_series, dir_series
L0195:     @staticmethod
L0196:     def _calc_adx(df: pd.DataFrame, period: int = 14):
L0197:         h, l, c = df["high"], df["low"], df["close"]
L0198:         tr = pd.concat([
L0199:             h - l,
L0200:             (h - c.shift()).abs(),
L0201:             (l - c.shift()).abs(),
L0202:         ], axis=1).max(axis=1)
L0203:         dm_plus  = (h - h.shift()).clip(lower=0).where(
L0204:             (h - h.shift()) > (l.shift() - l), 0
L0205:         )
L0206:         dm_minus = (l.shift() - l).clip(lower=0).where(
L0207:             (l.shift() - l) > (h - h.shift()), 0
L0208:         )
L0209:         atr14    = tr.ewm(span=period, adjust=False).mean()
L0210:         di_plus  = 100 * dm_plus.ewm(span=period, adjust=False).mean() / (atr14 + 1e-10)
L0211:         di_minus = 100 * dm_minus.ewm(span=period, adjust=False).mean() / (atr14 + 1e-10)
L0212:         dx       = 100 * (di_plus - di_minus).abs() / (di_plus + di_minus + 1e-10)
L0213:         adx_val  = dx.ewm(span=period, adjust=False).mean()
L0214:         return adx_val, di_plus, di_minus
L0215:     def get_multi_tf_signal(self, market: str) -> Dict:
L0216:         signals = {}
L0217:         for tf in ["5", "60", "1440"]:
L0218:             df = self.get_cached(market, tf)
L0219:             if df is not None and not df.empty:
L0220:                 last = df.iloc[-1]
L0221:                 signals[tf] = {
L0222:                     "trend":       "UP" if last["close"] > last["ema200"] else "DOWN",
L0223:                     "rsi":         last["rsi"],
L0224:                     "macd_bull":   last["macd"] > last["macd_signal"],
L0225:                     "supertrend":  "UP" if last["supertrend_dir"] > 0 else "DOWN",
L0226:                 }
L0227:         return signals

L0006:   - NpyCache 연동: 부팅 시 NVMe → RAM 워밍업

L0021:       L1: Python dict (ns 접근)   ← 현재가, 최신 신호
L0022:       L2: numpy array (μs 접근)  ← OHLCV + 지표 전량

L0031:         self.orderbook_cache: Dict[str, dict]                = {}
L0032:         self.candle_cache: Dict[str, Dict[str, deque]] = defaultdict(
L0033:             lambda: defaultdict(lambda: deque(maxlen=max_candles))
L0034:         )

L0036:             lambda: deque(maxlen=max_ticks)
L0037:         )
L0038:         self._ttl_cache: Dict[str, Dict] = {}

L0043:         except Exception as e:
L0044:             self._npy_cache = None
L0045:             logger.debug(f"NpyCache 연동 실패 (무시): {e}")
L0046:         logger.info(
L0047:             f"✅ CacheManager 초기화 | "
L0048:             f"캔들={max_candles}/코인 | 틱={max_ticks}/코인 | "
L0049:             f"추정 메모리≈{self._estimate_memory_mb():.0f}MB"
L0050:         )
L0051:     def set_price(self, market: str, price: float):
L0052:         self.price_cache[market] = (price, time.time())
L0053:     def get_price(self, market: str, max_age: float = 5.0) -> Optional[float]:
L0054:         if market not in self.price_cache:
L0055:             return None
L0056:         price, ts = self.price_cache[market]
L0057:         if time.time() - ts > max_age:
L0058:             return None
L0059:         return price
L0060:     def get_all_prices(self) -> Dict[str, float]:
L0061:         now = time.time()
L0062:         return {
L0063:             m: p for m, (p, ts) in self.price_cache.items()
L0064:             if now - ts <= 10.0
L0065:         }
L0066:     def add_tick(self, market: str, tick: dict):
L0067:         self.tick_cache[market].append({
L0068:             "price":    tick.get("trade_price", 0),
L0069:             "volume":   tick.get("trade_volume", 0),
L0070:             "timestamp": tick.get("timestamp", time.time()),
L0071:             "ask_bid":  tick.get("ask_bid", ""),
L0072:         })
L0073:     def get_recent_ticks(self, market: str, n: int = 100) -> List[dict]:
L0074:         ticks = list(self.tick_cache[market])
L0075:         return ticks[-n:] if len(ticks) >= n else ticks
L0076:     def get_tick_vwap(self, market: str, n: int = 200) -> float:
L0077:         ticks = self.get_recent_ticks(market, n)
L0078:         if not ticks:
L0079:             return 0.0
L0080:         prices  = np.array([t["price"]  for t in ticks])
L0081:         volumes = np.array([t["volume"] for t in ticks])
L0082:         total   = volumes.sum()
L0083:         return float((prices * volumes).sum() / total) if total > 0 else float(prices.mean())
L0084:     def get_buy_sell_ratio(self, market: str, n: int = 100) -> float:
L0085:         ticks    = self.get_recent_ticks(market, n)
L0086:         if not ticks:
L0087:             return 1.0
L0088:         buy_vol  = sum(t["volume"] for t in ticks if t["ask_bid"] == "BID")
L0089:         sell_vol = sum(t["volume"] for t in ticks if t["ask_bid"] == "ASK")
L0090:         return buy_vol / (sell_vol + 1e-10)
L0091:     def set_orderbook(self, market: str, orderbook: dict):
L0092:         self.orderbook_cache[market] = orderbook
L0093:     def get_orderbook(self, market: str) -> Optional[dict]:
L0094:         return self.orderbook_cache.get(market)
L0095:     def get_bid_ask_spread(self, market: str) -> Optional[float]:
L0096:         ob    = self.orderbook_cache.get(market)
L0097:         if not ob:
L0098:             return None
L0099:         units = ob.get("orderbook_units", [])
L0100:         if not units:
L0101:             return None
L0102:         best_ask = units[0].get("ask_price", 0)
L0103:         best_bid = units[0].get("bid_price", 0)
L0104:         if best_ask > 0:
L0105:             return (best_ask - best_bid) / best_ask * 100
L0106:         return None
L0107:     def set_signal(self, market: str, signal: dict):
L0108:         self.signal_cache[market] = {**signal, "timestamp": time.time()}
L0109:     def get_signal(self, market: str, max_age: float = 300) -> Optional[dict]:
L0110:         sig = self.signal_cache.get(market)
L0111:         if sig and time.time() - sig.get("timestamp", 0) <= max_age:
L0112:             return sig
L0113:         return None
L0114:     def set(self, key: str, value: Any, ttl: float = 60.0):
L0115:         self._ttl_cache[key] = {"value": value, "expires": time.time() + ttl}
L0116:     def get(self, key: str) -> Optional[Any]:
L0117:         item = self._ttl_cache.get(key)
L0118:         if item and time.time() < item["expires"]:
L0119:             return item["value"]
L0120:         self._ttl_cache.pop(key, None)
L0121:         return None
L0122:     def warmup_from_npy(self, markets: List[str], timeframes: List[str] = None):
L0123:         """
L0124:         ✅ Step 2: 부팅 시 NVMe 캐시 → RAM 워밍업
L0125:         Crucial E100 NVMe → DDR5 RAM 전송
L0126:         """
L0127:         if self._npy_cache is None:
L0128:             return
L0129:         if timeframes is None:
L0130:             timeframes = ["60", "1440"]
L0131:         loaded = 0
L0132:         for market in markets:
L0133:             for tf in timeframes:
L0134:                 if self._npy_cache.is_fresh(market, tf, max_age_seconds=3600):
L0135:                     df = self._npy_cache.load(market, tf)
L0136:                     if df is not None and not df.empty:
L0137:                         for _, row in df.iterrows():
L0138:                             self.candle_cache[market][tf].append(row.to_dict())
L0139:                         loaded += 1
L0140:                         logger.debug(
L0141:                             f"⚡ NVMe→RAM 워밍업: {market}/{tf} | {len(df)}행"
L0142:                         )
L0143:         if loaded > 0:
L0144:             logger.info(
L0145:                 f"✅ NVMe 캐시 워밍업 완료: {loaded}개 마켓/타임프레임 로드"
L0146:             )
L0147:     def save_to_npy(self, market: str, timeframe: str, df):
L0148:         """pandas DataFrame을 NpyCache에 비동기 저장"""
L0149:         if self._npy_cache is None or df is None:
L0150:             return
L0151:         try:
L0152:             self._npy_cache.save(market, timeframe, df)
L0153:         except Exception as e:
L0154:             logger.debug(f"NpyCache 저장 실패 ({market}/{timeframe}): {e}")
L0155:     def _estimate_memory_mb(self) -> float:
L0156:         """캐시 예상 메모리 사용량 (MB) 추정"""
L0157:         max_c       = self.settings.database.cache_max_candles
L0158:         markets     = len(self.settings.trading.target_markets)
L0159:         candle_mb   = markets * max_c * 200 / 1e6
L0160:         tick_mb     = markets * self.settings.database.cache_max_ticks * 64 / 1e6
L0161:         return candle_mb + tick_mb
L0162:     def get_memory_usage_mb(self) -> float:
L0163:         """실제 메모리 사용량 (MB)"""
L0164:         try:
L0165:             import psutil, os
L0166:             proc = psutil.Process(os.getpid())
L0167:             return proc.memory_info().rss / 1e6
L0168:         except Exception:
L0169:             return 0.0
L0170:     def get_ohlcv(self, market: str, interval: str = "1h"):
L0171:         """NpyCache에서 OHLCV DataFrame 반환. 없으면 None."""
L0172:         try:
L0173:             npy = getattr(self, '_npy_cache', None)
L0174:             if npy is not None:
L0175:                 if hasattr(npy, 'load'):
L0176:                     df = npy.load(market, interval)
L0177:                 elif hasattr(npy, 'get'):
L0178:                     df = npy.get(market, interval)
L0179:                 else:
L0180:                     df = None
L0181:                 if df is not None and len(df) > 0:
L0182:                     return df
L0183:         except Exception:
L0184:             pass
L0185:         return None
L0186:     def get_candles(self, market: str, interval: str = "1h"):

L0188:         return self.get_ohlcv(market, interval)
L0189:     def set_ohlcv(self, market: str, interval: str, df) -> None:
L0190:         """NpyCache에 OHLCV DataFrame 저장."""

L0193:             if npy is not None:
L0194:                 if hasattr(npy, 'save'):
L0195:                     npy.save(market, interval, df)
L0196:                 elif hasattr(npy, 'set'):

L0198:         except Exception:
L0199:             pass
L0200:     def get_stats(self) -> dict:
L0201:         total_ticks = sum(len(v) for v in self.tick_cache.values())

L0037:                 "BTC": 0.0,
L0038:                 "ETH": 0.0,
L0039:             }
L0040:             logger.info("📝 페이퍼 트레이딩 모드 시작 (초기 자본: ₩1,000,000)")
L0041:         else:

L0050:     @async_retry(max_attempts=3, delay=0.5)
L0051:     async def get_balance(self, currency: str = "KRW") -> float:
L0052:         """잔고 조회"""
L0053:         await self._rest_limiter.acquire()
L0054:         if self.is_paper:
L0055:             return self._paper_balance.get(currency, 0.0)
L0056:         try:
L0057:             return self._upbit.get_balance(currency) or 0.0
L0058:         except Exception as e:

L0060:             return 0.0

L0067:         try:

L0070:         except Exception as e:

L0074:     async def get_current_price(self, market: str) -> Optional[float]:

L0081:                     return float(price) if price else None
L0082:                 except Exception:
L0083:                     return None

L0085:         try:
L0086:             price = pyupbit.get_current_price(market)
L0087:             return float(price) if price else None
L0088:         except Exception as e:
L0089:             logger.error(f"현재가 조회 실패 ({market}): {e}")

L0091:     @async_retry(max_attempts=3, delay=1.0)
L0092:     async def get_ohlcv(self, market: str, interval: str = "minute60",

L0104:     @async_retry(max_attempts=3, delay=1.0)
L0105:     async def buy_limit_order(self, market: str, price: float,
L0106:                               amount_krw: float) -> Optional[Dict]:
L0107:         """지정가 매수 주문"""
L0108:         await self._order_limiter.acquire()

L0116:                 logger.info(f"🟢 매수 주문 접수 | {market} | {price:,} × {volume:.8f}")
L0117:                 return result
L0118:             logger.error(f"매수 주문 실패: {result}")
L0119:             return None
L0120:         except Exception as e:
L0121:             logger.error(f"매수 주문 예외 ({market}): {e}")
L0122:             return None
L0123:     @async_retry(max_attempts=3, delay=1.0)
L0124:     async def buy_market_order(self, market: str, amount_krw: float) -> Optional[Dict]:
L0125:         """시장가 매수"""
L0126:         await self._order_limiter.acquire()
L0127:         price = await self.get_current_price(market)
L0128:         if not price:
L0129:             return None

L0134:             if result and "uuid" in result:

L0038:     """주문 실행 결과"""
L0039:     request: ExecutionRequest
L0040:     status: OrderStatus

L0043:     executed_volume: float = 0.0
L0044:     fee: float = 0.0
L0045:     timestamp: float = field(default_factory=time.time)
L0046:     error_message: str = ""
L0047:     @property

L0049:         return self.executed_price * self.executed_volume
L0050: class OrderExecutor:
L0051:     """
L0052:     주문 실행 엔진
L0053:     - 지정가 우선, 미체결 시 시장가 전환
L0054:     - 최대 3회 재시도
L0055:     - 체결 확인 (최대 60초 대기)
L0056:     - 슬리피지 추정
L0057:     """
L0058:     FILL_TIMEOUT = 60
L0059:     FILL_CHECK_INTERVAL = 2
L0060:     MAX_RETRIES = 3
L0061:     def __init__(self, adapter: UpbitAdapter, db_manager=None):
L0062:         self.adapter = adapter
L0063:         self.db_manager = db_manager
L0064:         self.settings = get_settings()
L0065:         self._active_orders: Dict[str, ExecutionResult] = {}
L0066:         self._execution_history: List[ExecutionResult] = []
L0067:         self._lock = asyncio.Lock()
L0068:     async def execute(self, request: ExecutionRequest) -> ExecutionResult:
L0069:         """주문 실행 (메인 진입점)"""
L0070:         logger.info(
L0071:             f"📤 주문 요청 | {request.market} | {request.side.name} | "
L0072:             f"금액={request.amount_krw:,.0f}KRW | 사유={request.reason}"
L0073:         )
L0074:         result = ExecutionResult(request=request, status=OrderStatus.PENDING)
L0075:         for attempt in range(self.MAX_RETRIES):
L0076:             try:
L0077:                 result = await self._execute_market(request)
L0078:                 if result.status in (OrderStatus.FILLED, OrderStatus.PARTIAL):
L0079:                     break
L0080:                 elif result.status == OrderStatus.FAILED:
L0081:                     if attempt < self.MAX_RETRIES - 1:
L0082:                         wait = 2 ** attempt
L0083:                         logger.warning(f"⚠️ 재시도 {attempt+1}/{self.MAX_RETRIES} ({wait}s 후)")
L0084:                         await asyncio.sleep(wait)
L0085:             except Exception as e:
L0086:                 logger.error(f"주문 실행 예외 (시도 {attempt+1}): {e}")
L0087:                 result.error_message = str(e)
L0088:                 if attempt == self.MAX_RETRIES - 1:
L0089:                     result.status = OrderStatus.FAILED
L0090:         self._execution_history.append(result)
L0091:         self._log_execution_result(result)
L0092:         return result
L0093:     async def _execute_limit(self, req: ExecutionRequest) -> ExecutionResult:
L0094:         """지정가 주문 실행 + 체결 대기"""
L0095:         result = ExecutionResult(request=req, status=OrderStatus.SUBMITTED)
L0096:         if req.side == OrderSide.BUY:
L0097:             order = await self.adapter.buy_limit_order(
L0098:                 req.market, req.limit_price, req.amount_krw
L0099:             )
L0100:         else:
L0101:             order = await self.adapter.sell_limit_order(
L0102:                 req.market, req.limit_price, req.volume
L0103:             )
L0104:         if not order or "error" in order:
L0105:             result.status = OrderStatus.FAILED
L0106:             result.error_message = str(order)
L0107:             return result
L0108:         result.order_uuid = order.get("uuid", "")
L0109:         async with self._lock:
L0110:             self._active_orders[result.order_uuid] = result
L0111:         filled = await self._wait_for_fill(result.order_uuid)
L0112:         if filled:
L0113:             result.status = OrderStatus.FILLED
L0114:             result.executed_price = float(filled.get("price", req.limit_price))
L0115:             result.executed_volume = float(filled.get("executed_volume", 0))
L0116:             result.fee = float(filled.get("fee", filled.get("paid_fee", 0)))
L0117:         else:
L0118:             logger.warning(f"⏱️ 체결 타임아웃 → 주문 취소 후 시장가 전환")
L0119:             await self.adapter.cancel_order(result.order_uuid)
L0120:             market_req = ExecutionRequest(
L0121:                 market=req.market, side=req.side,
L0122:                 amount_krw=req.amount_krw, volume=req.volume,
L0123:                 reason=req.reason + " (시장가 전환)"
L0124:             )
L0125:             return await self._execute_market(market_req)
L0126:         async with self._lock:
L0127:             self._active_orders.pop(result.order_uuid, None)
L0128:         return result
L0129:     async def _execute_market(self, req: ExecutionRequest) -> ExecutionResult:
L0130:         """시장가 주문 즉시 실행"""
L0131:         result = ExecutionResult(request=req, status=OrderStatus.SUBMITTED)
L0132:         if req.side == OrderSide.BUY:
L0133:             order = await self.adapter.buy_market_order(req.market, req.amount_krw)
L0134:         else:
L0135:             order = await self.adapter.sell_market_order(req.market, req.volume)
L0136:         if not order or "error" in order:
L0137:             result.status = OrderStatus.FAILED
L0138:             result.error_message = str(order)
L0139:             return result
L0140:         result.order_uuid = order.get("uuid", "")
L0141:         result.status = OrderStatus.FILLED
L0142:         result.executed_volume = float(order.get("executed_volume", 0))
L0143:         result.fee = float(order.get("fee", order.get("paid_fee", 0)))
L0144:         result.executed_price = float(order.get("price", 0))
L0145:         if result.executed_volume > 0 and result.executed_price == 0:
L0146:             current_price = await self.adapter.get_current_price(req.market)
L0147:             if current_price:
L0148:                 slippage = self.settings.trading.slippage_rate
L0149:                 result.executed_price = current_price * (1 + slippage if req.side == OrderSide.BUY else 1 - slippage)
L0150:         return result
L0151:     async def _wait_for_fill(self, order_uuid: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
L0152:         """체결될 때까지 대기 (최대 FILL_TIMEOUT초)"""
L0153:         start = time.time()
L0154:         while time.time() - start < self.FILL_TIMEOUT:
L0155:             await asyncio.sleep(self.FILL_CHECK_INTERVAL)
L0156:             order = await self.adapter.get_order(order_uuid)
L0157:             if not order:
L0158:                 continue
L0159:             state = order.get("state", "")
L0160:             if state == "done":
L0161:                 return order
L0162:             elif state in ("cancel", "cancelled"):
L0163:                 return None
L0164:         return None
L0165:     async def emergency_sell_all(self, market: str, reason: str = "긴급 청산") -> ExecutionResult:
L0166:         """보유 코인 전량 시장가 청산"""

L0176:         req = ExecutionRequest(
L0177:             market=market,
L0178:             side=OrderSide.SELL,
L0179:             amount_krw=0,
L0180:             volume=volume,
L0181:             reason=reason,
L0182:         )
L0183:         logger.warning(f"🚨 긴급 청산 실행 | {market} | {volume:.8f} | {reason}")

L0185:     async def cancel_all_orders(self, market: str = None) -> int:
L0186:         """미체결 주문 전체 취소"""

L0195:     def get_execution_stats(self) -> Dict:

L0198:             return {}
L0199:         filled = [r for r in self._execution_history if r.status == OrderStatus.FILLED]
L0200:         failed = [r for r in self._execution_history if r.status == OrderStatus.FAILED]
L0201:         return {

L0203:             "filled": len(filled),
L0204:             "failed": len(failed),
L0205:             "success_rate": len(filled) / len(self._execution_history) * 100,
L0206:             "total_fee": sum(r.fee for r in filled),
L0207:         }
L0208:     def _log_execution_result(self, result: ExecutionResult):
L0209:         """실행 결과 로깅 + DB 저장"""
L0210:         if result.status == OrderStatus.FILLED:
L0211:             logger.success(
L0212:                 f"✅ 체결 완료 | {result.request.market} | "
L0213:                 f"{result.request.side.name} | 체결가={result.executed_price:,.0f} | "
L0214:                 f"수량={result.executed_volume:.6f} | 수수료={result.fee:,.0f}KRW"
L0215:             )
L0216:         elif result.status == OrderStatus.FAILED:

L0001: """
L0002: Apex Bot - 실전 전환 안전장치 (M2)
L0003: 페이퍼 → 실거래 전환 전 모든 조건 검증
L0004: """
L0005: import os
L0006: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
L0007: from typing import Tuple, List, Dict
L0008: from datetime import datetime
L0009: from loguru import logger
L0010: @dataclass
L0011: class LiveGuardConfig:
L0012:     min_win_rate:        float = 0.50
L0013:     min_sharpe:          float = 0.50
L0014:     max_mdd:             float = 0.10
L0015:     min_expectancy:      float = 0.001
L0016:     min_trade_days:      int   = 14
L0017:     min_total_trades:    int   = 20
L0018:     max_first_order_krw: float = 50_000
L0019:     require_telegram:    bool  = True
L0020: @dataclass
L0021: class LiveGuardReport:
L0022:     passed:      bool         = False
L0023:     score:       float        = 0.0
L0024:     checks:      List[Dict]   = field(default_factory=list)
L0025:     advice:      List[str]    = field(default_factory=list)
L0026:     checked_at:  str          = ""
L0027: class LiveGuard:
L0028:     """실전 전환 안전장치"""
L0029:     def __init__(self, config: LiveGuardConfig = None):
L0030:         self.cfg = config or LiveGuardConfig()
L0031:         self._emergency_stop = False
L0032:         logger.info("✅ LiveGuard 초기화")
L0033:     def check_readiness(self, stats: Dict) -> LiveGuardReport:
L0034:         """
L0035:         stats 예시:
L0036:           { "win_rate": 0.55, "sharpe": 0.8, "mdd": -0.07,
L0037:             "expectancy": 0.003, "trade_days": 20,
L0038:             "total_trades": 35, "telegram_ok": True }
L0039:         """
L0040:         report = LiveGuardReport(checked_at=datetime.now().isoformat())
L0041:         checks = []
L0042:         def chk(name, value, threshold, higher_better=True, weight=1.0):
L0043:             ok = (value >= threshold) if higher_better else (value <= threshold)
L0044:             checks.append({
L0045:                 "name": name, "value": value,
L0046:                 "threshold": threshold, "ok": ok, "weight": weight
L0047:             })
L0048:             return ok
L0049:         chk("승률",           stats.get("win_rate",     0), self.cfg.min_win_rate,     weight=0.25)
L0050:         chk("샤프비율",       stats.get("sharpe",       0), self.cfg.min_sharpe,       weight=0.25)
L0051:         chk("최대낙폭",       abs(stats.get("mdd",      0)), self.cfg.max_mdd, False,  weight=0.20)
L0052:         chk("기대값",         stats.get("expectancy",   0), self.cfg.min_expectancy,   weight=0.15)
L0053:         chk("거래일수",       stats.get("trade_days",   0), self.cfg.min_trade_days,   weight=0.10)
L0054:         chk("총 거래수",      stats.get("total_trades", 0), self.cfg.min_total_trades, weight=0.05)
L0055:         if self.cfg.require_telegram:
L0056:             chk("텔레그램 설정", int(stats.get("telegram_ok", False)), 1, weight=0.0)
L0057:         report.checks = checks
L0058:         passed_weights = sum(c["weight"] for c in checks if c["ok"])
L0059:         total_weights  = sum(c["weight"] for c in checks)
L0060:         report.score   = passed_weights / total_weights if total_weights > 0 else 0
L0061:         report.passed  = all(c["ok"] for c in checks)
L0062:         if not report.passed:
L0063:             for c in checks:
L0064:                 if not c["ok"]:
L0065:                     report.advice.append(
L0066:                         f"⚠️  {c['name']}: 현재={c['value']:.3f} → "
L0067:                         f"필요={c['threshold']:.3f}"
L0068:                     )
L0069:         logger.info(
L0070:             f"실전 전환 검증: {'✅ 통과' if report.passed else '❌ 미통과'} "
L0071:             f"(점수={report.score:.1%})"
L0072:         )
L0073:         return report
L0074:     def emergency_stop(self) -> bool:
L0075:         self._emergency_stop = True
L0076:         logger.critical("🚨 EMERGENCY STOP 발동 — 모든 포지션 즉시 청산 요청")
L0077:         return True
L0078:     def is_emergency(self) -> bool:
L0079:         return self._emergency_stop
L0080:     def validate_order(self, amount_krw: float, is_live: bool) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
L0081:         if not is_live:
L0082:             return True, "페이퍼 모드 — 검증 불필요"
L0083:         if amount_krw > self.cfg.max_first_order_krw:
L0084:             return False, (
L0085:                 f"실거래 주문 한도 초과: "
L0086:                 f"₩{amount_krw:,.0f} > ₩{self.cfg.max_first_order_krw:,.0f}"
L0087:             )
L0088:         return True, f"주문 금액 검증 통과: ₩{amount_krw:,.0f}"
L0089:     def summary(self, report: LiveGuardReport) -> str:
L0090:         lines = [
L0091:             f"\n{'='*50}",
L0092:             f"  실전 전환 적합성 검증",
L0093:             f"  점수: {report.score:.1%} | {'✅ 통과' if report.passed else '❌ 미통과'}",
L0094:             f"{'='*50}",
L0095:         ]
L0096:         for c in report.checks:
L0097:             icon = "✅" if c["ok"] else "❌"
L0098:             lines.append(f"  {icon} {c['name']}: {c['value']:.3f} (기준: {c['threshold']:.3f})")
L0099:         if report.advice:
L0100:             lines.append("\n  [개선 필요]")
L0101:             for a in report.advice:
L0102:                 lines.append(f"  {a}")
L0103:         lines.append("="*50)
L0104:         return "\n".join(lines)

FILE: core/smart_wallet.py  (23.1KB → 17.1KB)

L0001: from __future__ import annotations
L0002: """
L0003: SmartWallet v1.0
L0004: ════════════════
L0005: 코인 하나 = 하나의 독립 지갑.
L0006: 지갑 안에 Layer 0/1/2 로 수량을 분리 관리.
L0007: Layer 0 (HOLD)  : 장기보유. 절대 불가침.
L0008: Layer 1 (DUST)  : 짜투리. 단독 매도 안 함.
L0009:                   가격 상승 시 자동 SELLABLE 업그레이드.
L0010:                   매도 신호 강할 때 bot 합산 청산.
L0011: Layer 2 (BOT)   : 봇 트랜잭션 단위 추적.
L0012:                   매도 신호 강도에 따라 청산 비율 자동 결정.
L0013: 핵심 철학:
L0014:   - 짜투리는 "짐"이 아니라 "공짜 수량"으로 취급
L0015:   - 매도 시 항상 짜투리를 먼저 소진 (FIFO 역순)
L0016:   - 실거래 잔고와 매 사이클 동기화
L0017: """
L0018: import time
L0019: import json
L0020: from enum import Enum
L0021: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
L0022: from pathlib import Path
L0023: from typing import Optional
L0024: from loguru import logger
L0025: UPBIT_MIN_KRW  = 5_000
L0026: UPBIT_DEAD_KRW =   500
L0027: DUST_EXPIRE_DAYS = 30
L0028: class LayerType(Enum):
L0029:     HOLD = "HOLD"
L0030:     DUST = "DUST"
L0031:     BOT  = "BOT"
L0032:     DEAD = "DEAD"
L0033: class DustState(Enum):
L0034:     PENDING    = "PENDING"
L0035:     SELLABLE   = "SELLABLE"
L0036:     ORPHAN     = "ORPHAN"
L0037: @dataclass
L0038: class BotTransaction:
L0039:     """봇이 실행한 개별 매수 트랜잭션"""
L0040:     tx_id    : str
L0041:     qty      : float
L0042:     price    : float
L0043:     timestamp: float = field(default_factory=time.time)
L0044:     sold_qty : float = 0.0
L0045:     @property
L0046:     def remaining_qty(self) -> float:
L0047:         return max(0.0, self.qty - self.sold_qty)
L0048: @dataclass
L0049: class CoinWallet:
L0050:     """
L0051:     코인 하나의 완전한 지갑.
L0052:     Layer 0/1/2 를 모두 포함.
L0053:     """
L0054:     symbol: str
L0055:     hold_qty      : float = 0.0
L0056:     dust_qty      : float = 0.0
L0057:     dust_avg_price: float = 0.0
L0058:     dust_state    : DustState = DustState.PENDING
L0059:     dust_since    : float = field(default_factory=time.time)
L0060:     transactions  : list[BotTransaction] = field(default_factory=list)
L0061:     is_hold       : bool = False
L0062:     @property
L0063:     def bot_qty(self) -> float:
L0064:         return sum(tx.remaining_qty for tx in self.transactions)
L0065:     @property
L0066:     def bot_avg_price(self) -> float:
L0067:         txs = [tx for tx in self.transactions if tx.remaining_qty > 0]
L0068:         if not txs:
L0069:             return 0.0
L0070:         total_qty = sum(tx.remaining_qty for tx in txs)
L0071:         total_cost= sum(tx.remaining_qty * tx.price for tx in txs)
L0072:         return total_cost / total_qty if total_qty > 0 else 0.0
L0073:     @property
L0074:     def total_sellable_qty(self) -> float:
L0075:         """봇이 매도할 수 있는 전체 수량 (BOT + DUST 합산)"""
L0076:         return self.bot_qty + (
L0077:             self.dust_qty if self.dust_state != DustState.PENDING
L0078:             or self.bot_qty > 0
L0079:             else 0.0
L0080:         )
L0081:     def dust_value(self, current_price: float) -> float:
L0082:         return self.dust_qty * current_price
L0083:     def bot_value(self, current_price: float) -> float:
L0084:         return self.bot_qty * current_price
L0085:     def total_value(self, current_price: float) -> float:
L0086:         return (self.hold_qty + self.dust_qty + self.bot_qty) * current_price
L0087:     def refresh_dust_state(self, current_price: float):
L0088:         if self.dust_qty < 1e-10:
L0089:             return
L0090:         val  = self.dust_qty * current_price
L0091:         days = (time.time() - self.dust_since) / 86400
L0092:         if days >= DUST_EXPIRE_DAYS:
L0093:             if self.dust_state != DustState.ORPHAN:
L0094:                 self.dust_state = DustState.ORPHAN
L0095:                 logger.warning(
L0096:                     f"👻 {self.symbol}: 짜투리 {self.dust_qty:.8f}개 "
L0097:                     f"→ {days:.0f}일 방치 → 고아 포지션 지정"
L0098:                 )
L0099:         elif val >= UPBIT_MIN_KRW and self.dust_state == DustState.PENDING:
L0100:             self.dust_state = DustState.SELLABLE
L0101:             logger.info(
L0102:                 f"⬆️  {self.symbol}: 짜투리 ₩{val:,.0f} ≥ ₩{UPBIT_MIN_KRW:,} "
L0103:                 f"→ SELLABLE 업그레이드"
L0104:             )
L0105:     def __repr__(self):
L0106:         return (
L0107:             f"CoinWallet({self.symbol} | "
L0108:             f"hold={self.hold_qty:.6f} | "
L0109:             f"dust={self.dust_qty:.6f}[{self.dust_state.value}] | "
L0110:             f"bot={self.bot_qty:.6f} | "
L0111:             f"txs={len(self.transactions)})"
L0112:         )
L0113: class SmartSellDecider:
L0114:     """
L0115:     신호 강도 + 지갑 상태를 보고
L0116:     최적의 청산 수량과 방식을 결정.
L0117:     """
L0118:     @staticmethod
L0119:     def decide(
L0120:         wallet       : CoinWallet,
L0121:         current_price: float,
L0122:         confidence   : float,
L0123:     ) -> dict:
L0124:         """
L0125:         Returns:
L0126:             {
L0127:               "ok"        : bool,
L0128:               "qty"       : float,
L0129:               "strategy"  : str,
L0130:               "note"      : str,
L0131:               "includes_dust": bool,
L0132:             }
L0133:         """
L0134:         bot_qty  = wallet.bot_qty
L0135:         dust_qty = wallet.dust_qty
L0136:         hold_qty = wallet.hold_qty
L0137:         if wallet.is_hold and bot_qty < 1e-10:
L0138:             return {
L0139:                 "ok": False, "qty": 0.0,
L0140:                 "strategy": "HOLD_BLOCK",
L0141:                 "note": "🔒 HOLD 코인, BOT 수량 없음 → 차단",
L0142:                 "includes_dust": False,
L0143:             }
L0144:         if bot_qty < 1e-10:
L0145:             return {
L0146:                 "ok": False, "qty": 0.0,
L0147:                 "strategy": "NO_BOT_QTY",
L0148:                 "note": "BOT 보유 수량 없음",
L0149:                 "includes_dust": False,
L0150:             }
L0151:         include_dust = False
L0152:         dust_note    = ""
L0153:         if dust_qty > 1e-10:
L0154:             dust_val = dust_qty * current_price
L0155:             if dust_val < UPBIT_DEAD_KRW:
L0156:                 dust_note    = f"짜투리 ₩{dust_val:,.0f} 사망잔고 → 제외"
L0157:                 include_dust = False
L0158:             else:
L0159:                 include_dust = True
L0160:                 dust_note    = (
L0161:                     f"짜투리 {dust_qty:.8f}개(₩{dust_val:,.0f}) 합산 ✅"
L0162:                 )
L0163:         if confidence >= 0.80:
L0164:             qty      = bot_qty + (dust_qty if include_dust else 0.0)
L0165:             strategy = "FULL_EXIT"
L0166:             note     = f"강한 매도 신호({confidence:.0%}) → 전량 청산"
L0167:         elif confidence >= 0.55:
L0168:             qty      = bot_qty * 0.5 + (dust_qty if include_dust else 0.0)
L0169:             strategy = "HALF_EXIT"
L0170:             note     = f"중간 신호({confidence:.0%}) → 50% 청산"
L0171:         elif confidence >= 0.35:
L0172:             qty           = bot_qty * 0.25
L0173:             strategy      = "PARTIAL_EXIT"
L0174:             note          = f"약한 신호({confidence:.0%}) → 25% 청산"
L0175:             include_dust  = False
L0176:             dust_note     = "약한 신호 → 짜투리 보류 (더 좋은 기회 대기)"
L0177:         else:
L0178:             return {
L0179:                 "ok": False, "qty": 0.0,
L0180:                 "strategy": "HOLD_SIGNAL",
L0181:                 "note": f"신호 너무 약함({confidence:.0%}) → 보류",
L0182:                 "includes_dust": False,
L0183:             }
L0184:         value_krw = qty * current_price
L0185:         if value_krw < UPBIT_MIN_KRW:
L0186:             if dust_qty > 1e-10 and not include_dust:
L0187:                 qty          += dust_qty
L0188:                 include_dust  = True
L0189:                 value_krw     = qty * current_price
L0190:                 dust_note     = "최소금액 부족 → 짜투리 강제 합산"
L0191:             if value_krw < UPBIT_MIN_KRW:
L0192:                 return {
L0193:                     "ok": False, "qty": 0.0,
L0194:                     "strategy": "MIN_ORDER_FAIL",
L0195:                     "note": (
L0196:                         f"₩{value_krw:,.0f} < ₩{UPBIT_MIN_KRW:,} "
L0197:                         f"→ 매도 보류"
L0198:                     ),
L0199:                     "includes_dust": False,
L0200:                 }
L0201:         full_note = f"{note} | {dust_note}" if dust_note else note
L0202:         return {
L0203:             "ok"           : True,
L0204:             "qty"          : qty,
L0205:             "strategy"     : strategy,
L0206:             "note"         : full_note,
L0207:             "includes_dust": include_dust,
L0208:             "value_krw"    : value_krw,
L0209:             "confidence"   : confidence,
L0210:         }

L0243:         """

L0265:                 drift    = abs(actual - expected)
L0266:                 if drift > 1e-6:
L0267:                     logger.warning(
