L0291:     def predict(
L0292:         self, state: np.ndarray
L0293:     ) -> Tuple[Optional[str], float]:
L0294:         """
L0295:         현재 상태에서 행동 예측
L0296:         Args:
L0297:             state: 관측 벡터 (n_features,)
L0298:         Returns:
L0299:             (action_str, confidence)
L0300:             action_str: "BUY" / "HOLD" / "SELL"
L0301:             confidence: 0.0 ~ 1.0
L0302:         """
L0303:         if not self._is_trained or self._model is None:
L0304:             return None, 0.0
L0305:         try:
L0306:             action, _states = self._model.predict(
L0307:                 state.reshape(1, -1), deterministic=True
L0308:             )
L0309:             action = int(action)
L0310:             obs_tensor = self._model.policy.obs_to_tensor(
L0311:                 state.reshape(1, -1)
L0312:             )[0]
L0313:             with (torch.no_grad() if TORCH_AVAILABLE else _no_grad_ctx()):
L0314:                 dist = self._model.policy.get_distribution(obs_tensor)
L0315:                 probs = dist.distribution.probs.cpu().numpy()[0]
L0316:             confidence = float(probs[action])
L0317:             action_map = {0: "HOLD", 1: "BUY", 2: "SELL"}
L0318:             return action_map[action], confidence
L0319:         except Exception as e:
L0320:             logger.debug(f"PPO predict 오류: {e}")
L0321:             return None, 0.0

L0325:         """

L0339:                 "BUY":  SignalType.BUY,

L0341:                 "HOLD": SignalType.HOLD,
L0342:             }
L0343:             return {
L0344:                 "signal":     signal_map.get(action_str, SignalType.HOLD),
L0345:                 "confidence": confidence,
L0346:                 "source":     "PPO_RL",
L0347:                 "action":     action_str,
L0348:             }
L0349:         except Exception as e:

L0371:     def _evaluate(self, df: pd.DataFrame, n_episodes: int = 3) -> Dict:
L0372:         """검증 데이터로 성과 평가"""
L0373:         if not (GYM_AVAILABLE and SB3_AVAILABLE and self._model):
L0374:             return {}
L0375:         all_pnls = []
L0376:         all_wins = []
L0377:         all_trades = []
L0378:         for _ in range(n_episodes):
L0379:             env = TradingEnv(df)
L0380:             obs, _ = env.reset()
L0381:             done = False
L0382:             while not done:
L0383:                 action, _ = self._model.predict(obs, deterministic=True)
L0384:                 obs, _, terminated, truncated, _ = env.step(int(action))
L0385:                 done = terminated or truncated
L0386:             final_val = env.capital + env.position * float(df["close"].iloc[-1])
L0387:             pnl = (final_val / TradingEnv.INITIAL_CAPITAL - 1) * 100
L0388:             all_pnls.append(pnl)
L0389:             all_wins.append(env.win_count)
L0390:             all_trades.append(env.trade_count)
L0391:         avg_pnl = sum(all_pnls) / len(all_pnls)
L0392:         total_trades = sum(all_trades)
L0393:         total_wins = sum(all_wins)
L0394:         win_rate = (total_wins / total_trades * 100) if total_trades > 0 else 0
L0395:         pnl_series = pd.Series(all_pnls)
L0396:         sharpe = (pnl_series.mean() / pnl_series.std()) if pnl_series.std() > 0 else 0
L0397:         return {
L0398:             "pnl_pct": round(avg_pnl, 2),
L0399:             "win_rate": round(win_rate, 1),
L0400:             "trades": total_trades // n_episodes,
L0401:             "sharpe": round(sharpe, 3),
L0402:         }
L0403: def check_ppo_dependencies() -> Dict[str, bool]:
L0404:     """PPO 의존성 확인"""
L0405:     return {
L0406:         "gymnasium": GYM_AVAILABLE,
L0407:         "stable_baselines3": SB3_AVAILABLE,
L0408:         "torch": TORCH_AVAILABLE,
L0409:     }

L0412: PPO 에이전트 활성화 방법:
L0413:   pip install gymnasium stable-baselines3[extra] torch
L0414: GPU 가속 (RTX 5060):
L0415:   pip install torch torchvision --index-url https://download.pytorch.org/whl/cu128
L0416: """
L0417: class _no_grad_ctx:

L0419:     def __exit__(self, *_): pass

FILE: models/train/auto_trainer.py  (6.9KB → 5.6KB)

L0001: """
L0002: 매일 자동 재학습 파이프라인
L0003: - 데이터: 500개 캔들 (약 3주치 60분봉)
L0004: - 조건: 이전 모델 대비 val_acc 하락 없거나 RETRAIN_DAYS 경과
L0005: - 저장: models/saved/ensemble_best.pt (자동 교체)
L0006: - 실패시 이전 모델 자동 복원 (rollback)
L0007: """
L0008: import asyncio
L0009: import shutil
L0010: from datetime import datetime
L0011: from pathlib import Path
L0012: from typing import Optional
L0013: from utils.logger import logger
L0014: class AutoTrainer:
L0015:     """자동 재학습 파이프라인"""
L0016:     MODEL_PATH   = Path("models/saved/ensemble_best.pt")
L0017:     BACKUP_PATH  = Path("models/saved/ensemble_backup.pt")
L0018:     MIN_IMPROVE  = 0.005
L0019:     RETRAIN_DAYS = 3
L0020:     TRAIN_SCRIPT = "run_ml_train_v4.py"
L0021:     TIMEOUT_SEC  = 2400
L0022:     def __init__(self):
L0023:         self._last_retrain: Optional[datetime] = None
L0024:         self._last_val_acc: float = 0.0
L0025:         self._retrain_count: int  = 0
L0026:         self._is_training: bool   = False
L0027:     async def run_if_needed(self) -> bool:
L0028:         """
L0029:         재학습 필요 여부 확인 후 실행
L0030:         Returns: True if retrained successfully
L0031:         """
L0032:         if self._is_training:
L0033:             logger.warning("[AutoTrainer] 이미 학습 중 — 스킵")
L0034:             return False
L0035:         if not self._should_retrain():
L0036:             return False
L0037:         self._is_training = True
L0038:         try:
L0039:             logger.info("[AutoTrainer] 🔄 자동 재학습 시작...")
L0040:             return await self._retrain()
L0041:         finally:
L0042:             self._is_training = False
L0043:     def _should_retrain(self) -> bool:
L0044:         """재학습 필요 여부 판단"""
L0045:         now = datetime.now()
L0046:         if self._last_retrain is None:
L0047:             if not self.MODEL_PATH.exists():
L0048:                 logger.info("[AutoTrainer] 저장된 모델 없음 → 초기 학습")
L0049:                 return True
L0050:             return False
L0051:         elapsed_days = (now - self._last_retrain).days
L0052:         if elapsed_days >= self.RETRAIN_DAYS:
L0053:             logger.info(
L0054:                 f"[AutoTrainer] {elapsed_days}일 경과 "
L0055:                 f"(주기: {self.RETRAIN_DAYS}일) → 강제 재학습"
L0056:             )
L0057:             return True
L0058:         return False
L0059:     async def _retrain(self) -> bool:
L0060:         """실제 재학습 프로세스 실행"""
L0061:         import sys
L0062:         try:
L0063:             if self.MODEL_PATH.exists():
L0064:                 shutil.copy(self.MODEL_PATH, self.BACKUP_PATH)
L0065:                 logger.info(f"[AutoTrainer] 백업 완료: {self.BACKUP_PATH}")
L0066:             proc = await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec(
L0067:                 sys.executable, self.TRAIN_SCRIPT,
L0068:                 stdout=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
L0069:                 stderr=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
L0070:             )
L0071:             stdout, stderr = await asyncio.wait_for(
L0072:                 proc.communicate(), timeout=self.TIMEOUT_SEC
L0073:             )
L0074:             if proc.returncode != 0:
L0075:                 err_msg = stderr.decode(errors="replace")[-500:]
L0076:                 logger.error(f"[AutoTrainer] 재학습 실패 (returncode={proc.returncode}): {err_msg}")
L0077:                 self._rollback()
L0078:                 return False
L0079:             output  = stdout.decode(errors="replace")
L0080:             new_acc = self._parse_val_acc(output)
L0081:             logger.info(f"[AutoTrainer] 학습 완료 — val_acc={new_acc:.4f}")
L0082:             if (
L0083:                 self._last_val_acc > 0
L0084:                 and new_acc < self._last_val_acc - self.MIN_IMPROVE
L0085:             ):
L0086:                 logger.warning(
L0087:                     f"[AutoTrainer] 정확도 하락 감지 "
L0088:                     f"({self._last_val_acc:.4f} → {new_acc:.4f}) "
L0089:                     f"→ 이전 모델로 롤백"
L0090:                 )
L0091:                 self._rollback()
L0092:                 return False
L0093:             self._last_retrain  = datetime.now()
L0094:             self._last_val_acc  = new_acc
L0095:             self._retrain_count += 1
L0096:             logger.info(
L0097:                 f"[AutoTrainer] ✅ 재학습 성공 "
L0098:                 f"val_acc={new_acc:.4f} "
L0099:                 f"(총 {self._retrain_count}회)"
L0100:             )
L0101:             return True
L0102:         except asyncio.TimeoutError:
L0103:             logger.error(
L0104:                 f"[AutoTrainer] 타임아웃 ({self.TIMEOUT_SEC//60}분 초과) — 롤백"
L0105:             )
L0106:             self._rollback()
L0107:             return False
L0108:         except Exception as e:
L0109:             logger.error(f"[AutoTrainer] 예외 발생: {e}")
L0110:             self._rollback()
L0111:             return False
L0112:     def _rollback(self):
L0113:         """이전 모델 복원"""
L0114:         if self.BACKUP_PATH.exists():
L0115:             shutil.copy(self.BACKUP_PATH, self.MODEL_PATH)
L0116:             logger.info("[AutoTrainer] 🔄 이전 모델 복원 완료")
L0117:     @staticmethod
L0118:     def _parse_val_acc(output: str) -> float:
L0119:         """학습 출력 로그에서 val_acc 파싱"""
L0120:         import re
L0121:         patterns = [
L0122:             r"Val Acc[:\s]+([\d.]+)%",
L0123:             r"val_acc[=:\s]+([\d.]+)",
L0124:             r"Final.*?Acc[:\s]+([\d.]+)",
L0125:         ]
L0126:         for pat in patterns:
L0127:             m = re.search(pat, output, re.IGNORECASE)
L0128:             if m:
L0129:                 val = float(m.group(1))
L0130:                 return val / 100 if val > 1.0 else val
L0131:         return 0.0
L0132:     def get_status(self) -> dict:
L0133:         """현재 AutoTrainer 상태 반환"""
L0134:         return {
L0135:             "last_retrain":   self._last_retrain.isoformat() if self._last_retrain else "없음",
L0136:             "last_val_acc":   f"{self._last_val_acc*100:.2f}%",
L0137:             "retrain_count":  self._retrain_count,
L0138:             "is_training":    self._is_training,
L0139:             "next_retrain_in": (
L0140:                 f"{self.RETRAIN_DAYS - (datetime.now() - self._last_retrain).days}일"
L0141:                 if self._last_retrain else "다음 재시작 시"
L0142:             ),
L0143:         }

L0001: """
L0002: APEX BOT - 전략 기본 클래스 (Abstract Base Class)
L0003: 모든 전략이 상속하는 표준 인터페이스
L0004: """
L0005: from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
L0006: from dataclasses import dataclass
L0007: from datetime import datetime
L0008: from enum import Enum
L0009: from typing import Optional
L0010: import pandas as pd
L0011: import logging
L0012: logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
L0013: class SignalType(Enum):
L0014:     BUY  = 1
L0015:     HOLD = 0
L0016:     SELL = -1
L0017: @dataclass
L0018: class StrategySignal:
L0019:     """전략 신호 데이터"""
L0020:     strategy_name: str
L0021:     market: str
L0022:     signal: SignalType
L0023:     score: float
L0024:     confidence: float

L0027:     take_profit: float
L0028:     reason: str
L0029:     timeframe: str
L0030:     timestamp: datetime
L0031:     metadata: dict = None
L0032:     def __post_init__(self):
L0033:         if self.metadata is None:
L0034:             self.metadata = {}
L0035:     @property
L0036:     def is_buy(self) -> bool:
L0037:         return self.signal == SignalType.BUY
L0038:     @property
L0039:     def is_sell(self) -> bool:
L0040:         return self.signal == SignalType.SELL
L0041:     @property
L0042:     def weighted_score(self) -> float:
L0043:         """가중 점수 (신호값 × 신뢰도)"""
L0044:         return self.score * self.confidence
L0045:     @property
L0046:     def signal_type(self) -> 'SignalType':
L0047:         """하위 호환: signal 필드의 별칭"""
L0048:         return self.signal
L0049:     @property
L0050:     def strength(self) -> float:
L0051:         """하위 호환: score 필드의 별칭"""
L0052:         return self.score
L0053: Signal = StrategySignal
L0054: class BaseStrategy(ABC):
L0055:     """
L0056:     전략 추상 기본 클래스
L0057:     모든 전략 모듈이 이 클래스를 상속
L0058:     """
L0059:     NAME: str = "base"
L0060:     DESCRIPTION: str = ""
L0061:     WEIGHT: float = 1.0
L0062:     MIN_CANDLES: int = 200
L0063:     SUPPORTED_TIMEFRAMES: list = ["60"]
L0064:     def __init__(self, params: dict = None):
L0065:         self.params = params or self._default_params()
L0066:         self._last_signal: Optional[StrategySignal] = None
L0067:         self._signal_count = 0
L0068:         self._enabled = True
L0069:     @abstractmethod
L0070:     def _default_params(self) -> dict:
L0071:         """기본 파라미터 반환"""
L0072:         return {}
L0073:     @abstractmethod
L0074:     def generate_signal(self, df: pd.DataFrame, market: str,
L0075:                         timeframe: str = "60") -> Optional[StrategySignal]:
L0076:         """
L0077:         신호 생성 (핵심 메서드)
L0078:         Args:
L0079:             df: OHLCV + 지표 DataFrame (calculate_all_indicators 적용 완료)
L0080:             market: 마켓 코드 (예: "KRW-BTC")
L0081:             timeframe: 타임프레임 (분 단위)
L0082:         Returns:
L0083:             StrategySignal 또는 None (신호 없음)
L0084:         """
L0085:         pass
L0086:     def validate_df(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> bool:
L0087:         """DataFrame 유효성 검증"""
L0088:         if df is None or df.empty:
L0089:             return False
L0090:         if len(df) < self.MIN_CANDLES:
L0091:             logger.debug(f"⚠️ {self.NAME}: 캔들 부족 ({len(df)} < {self.MIN_CANDLES})")
L0092:             return False
L0093:         required_cols = ["open", "high", "low", "close", "volume"]
L0094:         missing = [c for c in required_cols if c not in df.columns]
L0095:         if missing:
L0096:             logger.warning(f"⚠️ {self.NAME}: 필수 컬럼 누락 {missing}")
L0097:             return False
L0098:         return True
L0099:     def _create_signal(
L0100:         self,

L0102:         score: float,

L0116:             market=market,

L0118:             score=score,
L0119:             confidence=min(max(confidence, 0.0), 1.0),
L0120:             entry_price=entry_price,

L0122:             take_profit=take_profit,
L0123:             reason=reason,
L0124:             timeframe=timeframe,
L0125:             timestamp=datetime.now(),

L0127:         )
L0128:         self._last_signal = sig
L0129:         logger.info(

L0131:             f"점수: {score:.2f} | 신뢰도: {confidence:.2%} | {reason}"
L0132:         )

FILE: strategies/order_block_detector.py  (7.9KB → 7.6KB)
============================================================
L0001: """
L0002: APEX BOT - 오더블록 탐지기 v1.0
L0003: 스마트머니 개념 기반 기관 매수/매도 흔적 탐지
L0004: ────────────────────────────────────────────
L0005: 정의:
L0006:   Bullish OB: 강한 상승 직전의 마지막 하락 캔들 (기관 매수 흔적)
L0007:   Bearish OB: 강한 하락 직전의 마지막 상승 캔들 (기관 매도 흔적)
L0008: 탐지 조건:
L0009:   1. 충격 이동: 이후 N캔들이 ATR의 2배 이상 이동
L0010:   2. OB 캔들:   이동 방향 반대 캔들 (몸통 ATR 10% 이상)
L0011:   3. 신선도:    이후 가격이 OB 영역 재진입 안 한 것만 유효
L0012:   4. 거리:      현재가 기준 2% 이내 OB만 활성 신호로 처리
L0013: """
L0014: from __future__ import annotations
L0015: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
L0016: from typing import Optional, List
L0017: import numpy as np
L0018: import pandas as pd
L0019: from loguru import logger
L0020: @dataclass
L0021: class OrderBlock:
L0022:     ob_type: str
L0023:     high: float
L0024:     low: float
L0025:     mid: float
L0026:     candle_idx: int
L0027:     strength: float
L0028:     impulse_atr: float
L0029: @dataclass
L0030: class OrderBlockSignal:
L0031:     nearest_bullish: Optional[OrderBlock] = None
L0032:     nearest_bearish: Optional[OrderBlock] = None
L0033:     price_in_bullish: bool = False
L0034:     price_in_bearish: bool = False
L0035:     dist_bullish_pct: float = 999.0
L0036:     dist_bearish_pct: float = 999.0
L0037:     signal: str = "NEUTRAL"
L0038:     confidence: float = 0.0
L0039:     ob_count: int = 0
L0040: class OrderBlockDetector:
L0041:     """
L0042:     오더블록 탐지기
L0043:     Parameters
L0044:     ----------
L0045:     impulse_mult : float  충격 이동 ATR 배수 (기본 2.0)
L0046:     lookback     : int    탐지 캔들 수 (기본 100)
L0047:     max_obs      : int    최대 유지 OB 수 (기본 5)
L0048:     """
L0049:     def __init__(
L0050:         self,
L0051:         impulse_mult: float = 2.0,
L0052:         lookback: int = 100,
L0053:         max_obs: int = 5,
L0054:     ):
L0055:         self.impulse_mult = impulse_mult
L0056:         self.lookback     = lookback
L0057:         self.max_obs      = max_obs
L0058:     def detect(self, df: pd.DataFrame, current_price: float) -> OrderBlockSignal:
L0059:         try:
L0060:             if df is None or len(df) < 30:
L0061:                 return OrderBlockSignal()
L0062:             df = df.tail(self.lookback).copy().reset_index(drop=True)
L0063:             df.columns = [c.lower() for c in df.columns]
L0064:             required = {"open", "high", "low", "close"}
L0065:             if not required.issubset(set(df.columns)):
L0066:                 return OrderBlockSignal()
L0067:             atr = self._calc_atr(df)
L0068:             if atr <= 0:
L0069:                 return OrderBlockSignal()
L0070:             bullish_obs, bearish_obs = [], []
L0071:             scan_end = len(df) - 3
L0072:             for i in range(5, scan_end):
L0073:                 ob = self._check_bullish(df, i, atr)
L0074:                 if ob:
L0075:                     bullish_obs.append(ob)
L0076:                 ob2 = self._check_bearish(df, i, atr)
L0077:                 if ob2:
L0078:                     bearish_obs.append(ob2)
L0079:             bullish_obs = [o for o in bullish_obs if self._is_fresh(o, df, current_price, "bullish")]
L0080:             bearish_obs = [o for o in bearish_obs if self._is_fresh(o, df, current_price, "bearish")]
L0081:             bullish_obs = sorted(bullish_obs, key=lambda x: x.strength, reverse=True)[:self.max_obs]
L0082:             bearish_obs = sorted(bearish_obs, key=lambda x: x.strength, reverse=True)[:self.max_obs]
L0083:             return self._build_signal(bullish_obs, bearish_obs, current_price)
L0084:         except Exception as e:
L0085:             logger.debug(f"오더블록 탐지 오류: {e}")
L0086:             return OrderBlockSignal()
L0087:     def _check_bullish(self, df: pd.DataFrame, i: int, atr: float) -> Optional[OrderBlock]:
L0088:         c = df.iloc[i]
L0089:         if c["close"] >= c["open"]:
L0090:             return None
L0091:         body = abs(c["open"] - c["close"])
L0092:         if body < atr * 0.1:
L0093:             return None
L0094:         impulse = self._find_impulse(df, i, "up", atr)
L0095:         if impulse is None:
L0096:             return None
L0097:         strength = min(1.0, impulse / (self.impulse_mult * atr))
L0098:         freshness = (i / len(df)) * 0.3 + 0.7
L0099:         return OrderBlock(
L0100:             ob_type="bullish",
L0101:             high=c["high"], low=c["low"],
L0102:             mid=(c["high"] + c["low"]) / 2,
L0103:             candle_idx=i,
L0104:             strength=round(strength * freshness, 4),
L0105:             impulse_atr=round(impulse / atr, 2),
L0106:         )
L0107:     def _check_bearish(self, df: pd.DataFrame, i: int, atr: float) -> Optional[OrderBlock]:
L0108:         c = df.iloc[i]
L0109:         if c["close"] <= c["open"]:
L0110:             return None
L0111:         body = abs(c["close"] - c["open"])
L0112:         if body < atr * 0.1:
L0113:             return None
L0114:         impulse = self._find_impulse(df, i, "down", atr)
L0115:         if impulse is None:
L0116:             return None
L0117:         strength = min(1.0, impulse / (self.impulse_mult * atr))
L0118:         freshness = (i / len(df)) * 0.3 + 0.7
L0119:         return OrderBlock(
L0120:             ob_type="bearish",
L0121:             high=c["high"], low=c["low"],
L0122:             mid=(c["high"] + c["low"]) / 2,
L0123:             candle_idx=i,
L0124:             strength=round(strength * freshness, 4),
L0125:             impulse_atr=round(impulse / atr, 2),
L0126:         )
L0127:     def _find_impulse(self, df, start, direction, atr) -> Optional[float]:
L0128:         threshold = atr * self.impulse_mult
L0129:         look_ahead = min(5, len(df) - start - 1)
L0130:         ref = df.iloc[start]["close"]
L0131:         for j in range(1, look_ahead + 1):
L0132:             curr = df.iloc[start + j]["close"]
L0133:             move = (curr - ref) if direction == "up" else (ref - curr)
L0134:             if move >= threshold:
L0135:                 return move
L0136:         return None
L0137:     def _is_fresh(self, ob, df, current_price, ob_type) -> bool:
L0138:         after = df.iloc[ob.candle_idx + 1:]
L0139:         if ob_type == "bullish":
L0140:             return not (after["low"] < ob.low).any()
L0141:         else:
L0142:             return not (after["high"] > ob.high).any()
L0143:     def _build_signal(self, bullish_obs, bearish_obs, price) -> OrderBlockSignal:
L0144:         sig = OrderBlockSignal(ob_count=len(bullish_obs) + len(bearish_obs))
L0145:         below = [o for o in bullish_obs if o.high <= price * 1.02]
L0146:         if below:
L0147:             nb = min(below, key=lambda o: price - o.mid)
L0148:             sig.nearest_bullish   = nb
L0149:             sig.dist_bullish_pct  = abs(price - nb.mid) / nb.mid * 100
L0150:             sig.price_in_bullish  = nb.low <= price <= nb.high
L0151:         above = [o for o in bearish_obs if o.low >= price * 0.98]
L0152:         if above:
L0153:             na = min(above, key=lambda o: o.mid - price)
L0154:             sig.nearest_bearish   = na
L0155:             sig.dist_bearish_pct  = abs(price - na.mid) / na.mid * 100
L0156:             sig.price_in_bearish  = na.low <= price <= na.high
L0157:         if sig.price_in_bullish and sig.nearest_bullish:
L0158:             sig.signal, sig.confidence = "BUY_ZONE", sig.nearest_bullish.strength
L0159:         elif sig.price_in_bearish and sig.nearest_bearish:
L0160:             sig.signal, sig.confidence = "SELL_ZONE", sig.nearest_bearish.strength
L0161:         elif sig.nearest_bullish and sig.dist_bullish_pct < 1.5:
L0162:             sig.signal, sig.confidence = "BUY_ZONE", sig.nearest_bullish.strength * 0.7
L0163:         elif sig.nearest_bearish and sig.dist_bearish_pct < 1.5:
L0164:             sig.signal, sig.confidence = "SELL_ZONE", sig.nearest_bearish.strength * 0.7
L0165:         else:
L0166:             sig.signal, sig.confidence = "NEUTRAL", 0.0
L0167:         return sig
L0168:     @staticmethod
L0169:     def _calc_atr(df: pd.DataFrame, period: int = 14) -> float:
L0170:         try:
L0171:             h = df["high"].values
L0172:             l = df["low"].values
L0173:             c = df["close"].values
L0174:             tr = np.maximum(h[1:] - l[1:],
L0175:                  np.maximum(np.abs(h[1:] - c[:-1]),
L0176:                             np.abs(l[1:] - c[:-1])))
L0177:             if len(tr) < period:
L0178:                 return float(np.mean(tr)) if len(tr) > 0 else 0.0
L0179:             return float(np.mean(tr[-period:]))
L0180:         except Exception:
L0181:             return 0.0
